# math-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [A hybrid Lagrangian-Hamiltonian framework and its application to conserved integrals and symmetry groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03487)
*Stephen C. Anco*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一个混合框架，统一了拉格朗日力学和哈密顿力学中诺特定理（Noether's theorem）关于对称性与守恒量对应关系的核心方面，并应用于局部刘维尔可积系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在突出并统一诺特对应关系（Noether correspondence）在拉格朗日力学（Lagrangian mechanics）和哈密顿力学（Hamiltonian mechanics）中对称性与守恒积分的最重要方面，为理解这一基本物理原理提供更清晰的框架。

Method: 开发了一个混合框架，采用现代形式的诺特定理（仅需运动方程，无需显式拉格朗日量），并用拉格朗日变量（Lagrangian variables）表述泊松括号（Poisson bracket）以表达对称性对守恒积分的作用。

Result: 阐明了点对称性（point symmetries）与动力学对称性（dynamical symmetries）的特征，统一处理了自治（autonomous）与非自治（non-autonomous）系统，并应用于局部刘维尔可积（locally Liouville integrable）动力系统。

Conclusion: 该框架能够找到此类系统的完整诺特对称群（complete Noether symmetry group），为研究对称性与守恒量关系提供了统一的理论工具。

Abstract: A hybrid framework is developed that highlights and unifies the most important aspects of the Noether correspondence between symmetries and conserved integrals in Lagrangian and Hamiltonian mechanics. Several main results are shown: (1) a modern form of Noether's theorem is presented that uses only the equations of motion, with no knowledge required of an explicit Lagrangian; (2) the Poisson bracket is formulated with Lagrangian variables and used to express the action of symmetries on conserved integrals; (3) features of point symmetries versus dynamical symmetries are clarified and explained; (4) both autonomous and non-autonomous systems are treated on an equal footing. These results are applied to dynamical systems that are locally Liouville integrable. In particular, they allow finding the complete Noether symmetry group of such systems.

</details>


### [2] [Translational dynamics of diatomic molecule in magnetic quadrupole trap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03898)
*Yurij Yaremko,Maria Przybylska,Andrzej J. Maciejewski*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了处于特定量子态的同核双原子分子在四极磁场中的平动运动，通过数值和解析方法证明了该哈密顿系统不可积，并展示了周期性、准周期性和混沌轨道等动力学行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解处于${}^3Σ$电子态、深束缚振动态和确定宇称旋转态的同核双原子分子在四极磁场中的平动动力学。这种势阱源于电子总自旋与核轨道角动量同磁场四极矩的相互作用。

Method: 采用经典方法处理分子平动，通过数值和解析方法研究质心动力学的哈密顿方程。使用氢分子基态振动数据，通过庞加莱截面（Poincaré section）方法分析全局动力学，识别周期性、准周期性和混沌轨道。

Result: 证明了该哈密顿系统不可积（non-integrable）。粒子轨道被限制在随能量增长的束缚区域内，但在低能量（<1.8 K）时运动被限制在几厘米的加工室中。对称轴和水平面上的运动方程解可用雅可比椭圆函数（Jacobi elliptic functions）表示。

Conclusion: 该研究系统揭示了特定量子态双原子分子在四极磁场中的复杂平动动力学特性，包括不可积性、能量相关的束缚区域以及不同能量尺度下的运动限制，为相关实验提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We study the translational motions of homonuclear diatomic molecules prepared in their ${}^3Σ$ electronic states, deeply bound vibrational states, and rotational states of well-defined parity. The trapping potential arises due to the interaction of the total spin of electrons and orbital angular momentum of nuclei with the trap's quadrupole magnetic field. The translational motion of a molecule is treated classically. We examine the Hamilton equations that govern the center of mass dynamics numerically and analytically. Using data of a hydrogen molecule at the ground vibrational state, we present global dynamics using the Poincaré section method and various types of trajectories: periodic, quasi-periodic and chaotic. We prove that the Hamiltonian system governing this motion is non-integrable. The particle's orbits are confined to a bound region of space that grows with energy, but for small energies (< 1.8 K), the motion is restricted to a processing chamber (a few centimetres).
  Solutions of equations of motion occurring on the symmetry axis and the horizontal plane are expressed in terms of Jacobi elliptic functions.

</details>

# math.PR [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [The Gaussian Wave for Graphs of Finite Cone Type](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04386)
*Amir Dembo,Theo McKenzie*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文证明，在满足温和扩展条件的有限锥型无限树上，唯一具有格林函数（Green's function）诱导协方差的典型过程是高斯波（Gaussian wave）。这推广了Backhausz和Szegedy关于无限正则树的结果，并应用于随机二分双正则图和配置模型的特征向量局部分布分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在推广Backhausz和Szegedy关于无限正则树的结果，将高斯波作为唯一典型过程的结论扩展到更广泛的无限树类别。研究动机源于理解随机图特征向量局部分布的渐近行为，特别是二分双正则图和配置模型等随机图模型。

Method: 通过将问题简化为分析过程与格林函数列的内积分布，该方法利用格林函数的列易于计算的特性。证明策略基于对满足温和扩展条件的有限锥型无限树进行一般化处理，而非仅限于正则树。

Result: 主要结果表明：对于满足温和扩展条件的有限锥型无限树，唯一具有格林函数诱导协方差的典型过程是高斯波。这一结果可直接应用于随机二分双正则图，证明其特征向量局部邻域分布必须逼近高斯波；对于包括随机提升（random lifts）在内的通用配置模型，从任意小谱窗口均匀选择的特征向量的局部分布同样收敛于高斯波。

Conclusion: 该研究成功将高斯波作为唯一典型过程的结论从无限正则树推广到更一般的有限锥型无限树类别。这一推广为分析随机图特征向量的局部统计性质提供了理论基础，特别是在二分双正则图和配置模型等随机图模型中，特征向量的局部分布必然收敛于高斯波。

Abstract: We show that for any infinite tree of finite cone type satisfying a mild expansion condition, the only typical process on its vertices with covariance induced by the Green's function is the Gaussian wave. This generalizes a result of Backhausz and Szegedy, who proved this for the infinite regular tree of degree $d\geq 3$. We do this by giving a reduction to a statement concerning the distribution of the inner product of our process with columns of the Green's function, which in turn are straightforward to calculate.
  As a consequence, for random bipartite biregular graphs, the distribution of local neighborhoods of eigenvectors must approximate the Gaussian wave. Moreover, for generic configuration models including random lifts, the local distribution of a uniformly chosen eigenvector from any arbitrarily small spectral window likewise converges to the Gaussian wave.

</details>

# cond-mat.supr-con [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Enhanced superconductivity in palladium hydrides by non-perturbative electron-phonon effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03492)
*Raffaello Bianco,Ion Errea*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了钯氢化物（palladium hydrides）中超导临界温度异常同位素效应的关键机制：非线性电子-声子耦合（non-linear electron-phonon coupling）的贡献至关重要，而传统微扰方法会破坏同位素异常并高估临界温度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钯氢化物表现出最大的超导同位素效应异常：用较重同位素取代氢反而增加超导临界温度。虽然通常将此归因于强非谐氢振动，但现有第一性原理处理仅通过声子重整化（phonon renormalization）纳入非谐效应，忽略了电子-声子相互作用顶点（electron-phonon interaction vertices）的非线性贡献。

Method: 研究采用基于离子介导电子-电子相互作用（ion-mediated electron-electron interaction）显式评估的非微扰框架（non-perturbative framework），使非谐效应能够在声子谱和相互作用顶点中得到一致处理。该方法应用于PdH和PdD体系。

Result: 该方法恢复了异常同位素效应，并将计算得到的临界温度与实验值显著改善地吻合。相比之下，简单包含高阶微扰项会导致定性失效：临界温度被高估且同位素异常消失。

Conclusion: 非线性电子-声子耦合在钯氢化物中至关重要，非微扰框架能够一致处理声子谱和相互作用顶点中的非谐效应，从而正确解释异常同位素效应并准确预测超导临界温度。

Abstract: Palladium hydrides exhibit the largest isotope-effect anomaly in superconductivity: replacing hydrogen with heavier isotopes increases the superconducting critical temperature. Although this behavior is commonly attributed to strong anharmonic hydrogen vibrations, \textit{ab initio} treatments have so far incorporated anharmonic effects only through phonon renormalization, neglecting non-linear contributions to the electron-phonon interaction vertices. While such approaches reproduce the anomalous isotope trend, they severely underestimate the critical temperatures. Here, we show that non-linear electron-phonon coupling is essential in palladium hydrides. A straightforward inclusion of higher-order perturbative terms leads to a qualitative breakdown: the critical temperature is overestimated and the isotope anomaly is lost. We therefore adopt a non-perturbative framework based on an explicit evaluation of the ion-mediated electron-electron interaction, enabling anharmonic effects to be treated consistently in both the phonon spectra and the interaction vertices. Applied to PdH and PdD, it restores the anomalous isotope effect and brings calculated critical temperatures into significantly improved agreement with experiments.

</details>


### [5] [Limited coincidence between ultrahigh-field superconductivity and line of metamagnetic endpoints in UTe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03500)
*Peter Czajka,Sylvia K. Lewin,Thomas Halloran,Corey E. Frank,Gicela Saucedo Salas,G. Timothy Noe,Sheng Ran,John Singleton,Nicholas P. Butch*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: UTe₂中磁化强度随磁场角度变化的测量显示，在ab平面内，磁化跳跃在偏离b轴约18°时消失。无接触电导率测量表明，类晕状高场超导区域延伸至ab平面，仅存在于亚稳相边界终止点附近极窄角度范围（<1°），且超出最高测量场73T。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究UTe₂中亚稳磁转变（metamagnetic transition）随磁场角度变化的演化规律，特别关注磁化跳跃的消失角度，以及高场超导区域与亚稳相边界之间的空间关系。

Method: 通过测量不同磁场角度下UTe₂的场依赖磁化强度，追踪磁化跳跃随磁场偏离b轴的演化。同时采用无接触电导率测量（contactless conductivity measurements）来确定高场超导区域的空间分布。

Result: 对于ab平面内的磁场取向，M_a和M_b的磁化跳跃在偏离b轴约18°时消失。高场超导区域呈类晕状延伸至ab平面，仅存在于亚稳相边界终止点附近极窄角度范围（<1°），且超出最高测量场73T。当磁场向c轴倾斜时，超导与亚稳相边界不再重合，呈现不同趋势。

Conclusion: UTe₂中亚稳磁转变具有强烈的角度依赖性，磁化跳跃在特定角度范围内消失。高场超导区域与亚稳相边界在ab平面内存在紧密但有限的空间关联，而在向c轴倾斜时两者解耦，表明超导与磁性序之间存在复杂的相互作用。

Abstract: The field-dependent magnetization of UTe$_2$ was measured through the metamagnetic transition at a variety of field angles, tracking how the step in magnetization evolves with fields tilted away from the $b$ axis. For fields oriented within the $ab$ plane, jumps in both $M_a$ and $M_b$ vanish approximately 18° away from the $b$ axis. From contactless conductivity measurements, we find that the halo-like high-field superconducting region extends to the $ab$ plane, where it exists only within a very narrow ($<$1°) angular range near the termination of the metamagnetic phase boundary and extends beyond the highest measured field of 73 T. As the field orientation tilts towards the $c$ axis, the superconducting and metamagnetic phase boundaries no longer coincide and exhibit distinct trends.

</details>

# gr-qc [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [Regular Bardeen Black Hole Solutions in Rastall Theory: A Gravitational Decoupling Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03377)
*M. Sharif,Malick Sallah*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究将引力解耦（gravitational decoupling）的广义技术应用于Bardeen黑洞，在Rastall理论框架下生成新的黑洞解。通过分解场方程并采用线性状态方程，构建了两个扩展模型，分析了其物理特性与热力学性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于将引力解耦技术应用于Bardeen黑洞，在Rastall理论框架下探索新的黑洞解。该方法旨在通过分解场方程并引入额外物质源，构建扩展的黑洞模型并分析其物理特性。

Method: 采用引力解耦（gravitational decoupling）的广义技术，将对应额外物质源的场方程分解为两组。第一组采用Bardeen黑洞的度规函数，第二组考虑物质的线性状态方程（linear equation of state）进行求解。通过整合两组解，构建了两个扩展模型。

Result: 两个模型均具有渐近平坦性（asymptotically flat），但违反了能量边界条件（energy bounds）。密度、径向压力和霍金温度（Hawking temperature）表现出一致且可接受的行为。通过比热（specific heat）和海森矩阵（Hessian matrix）分析，确认了热力学稳定性。

Conclusion: 研究成功在Rastall理论框架下生成了新的黑洞解，这些解具有渐近平坦性和可接受的热力学行为。虽然违反了能量边界条件，但通过热力学分析确认了系统的稳定性，为黑洞物理研究提供了新的理论模型。

Abstract: This research applies the generalized technique of gravitational decoupling to the Bardeen black hole, producing novel black hole solutions in the context of Rastall theory. We proceed by decomposition of the field equations corresponding to an additional matter source into two sets, for further considerations. The metric functions of the Bardeen black hole are adopted to specify the first set. The second one, which is subject to an extra source, is resolved considering a linear equation of state of matter. Through the integration of the solutions of these sets, we develop two expanded models and conduct an in-depth analysis of their distinct physical characteristics, governed by specific parameters. We investigate thermodynamic quantities like density, anisotropic pressure, energy bounds, asymptotic flatness, and thermodynamical properties like the Hawking temperature, entropy, and specific heat, etc. Both models are asymptotically flat but violate the energy bounds. Furthermore, the density, radial pressure, and Hawking temperature demonstrate consistent and acceptable behavior. Ultimately, the thermodynamic stability is affirmed through the analysis of specific heat and the Hessian matrix.

</details>


### [7] [Dark Energy from Entanglements with Mirror Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03385)
*Merab Gogberashvili,Tinatin Tsiskaridze*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于成对宇宙（pair-universe）框架的暗能量（dark energy）解决方案，其中宇宙作为时间反演（time-reversed）扇区的纠缠对（entangled pair）出现，通过全局零能量条件（global zero-energy condition）抵消真空能贡献，并将观测到的暗能量解释为可见宇宙与其镜像对应物之间的有效纠缠能量（effective entanglement energy）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机在于解决暗能量问题（dark energy problem），特别是真空能量贡献所需的极端精细调节（extreme fine-tuning）。作者旨在提供一个统一框架，可能同时解释暗能量和暗物质（dark matter）的起源。

Method: 研究方法基于成对宇宙框架，其中宇宙作为时间反演扇区的纠缠对出现。将宇宙常数（cosmological constant）视为由边界条件（boundary conditions）确定的积分常数（integration constant）而非基本参数，并在宇宙事件视界（cosmological event horizon）施加物理上合理的边界条件来推导宇宙学方程。

Result: 研究结果表明，通过全局零能量条件，两个扇区的真空能量贡献可以相互抵消。在宇宙事件视界施加边界条件后，获得的积分常数与观测到的暗能量密度（dark energy density）一致，表明暗能量源于可见宇宙与其镜像对应物之间的有效纠缠能量。

Conclusion: 平行镜像世界（parallel mirror world）场景提供了一个统一框架，可能同时解释暗能量和暗物质的起源。该框架将暗能量视为有效纠缠能量而非真空涨落（vacuum fluctuations）的产物，并通过边界条件自然确定宇宙常数，避免了精细调节问题。

Abstract: We investigate a possible resolution of the dark energy problem within a pair-universe framework, in which the Universe emerges as an entangled pair of time-reversed sectors. In this setting, a global zero-energy condition allows vacuum energy contributions from the two sectors to cancel, alleviating the need for extreme fine-tuning. We propose that the observed dark energy does not originate from vacuum fluctuations but instead arises as an effective entanglement energy between the visible universe and its mirror counterpart. Treating the cosmological constant as an integration constant fixed by boundary conditions rather than a fundamental parameter, we show that the cosmological equations can be formulated without explicitly introducing vacuum energy. By imposing physically motivated boundary conditions at the cosmological event horizon, we obtain an integration constant consistent with the observed dark energy density. The parallel mirror world scenario thus provides a unified framework that may simultaneously explain the origins of dark energy and dark matter.

</details>


### [8] [The perturbation solutions to the Blandford-Znajek mechanism in the Kerr-Sen black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03391)
*Haiyuan Feng,Ziqiang Cai,Rong-Jia Yang,Jinjun Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究通过微扰求解非线性Grad-Shafranov方程，分析了Kerr-Sen黑洞在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-伸缩子-轴子理论框架下的稳态轴对称无力磁层，发现伸缩子参数r₂能提升能量提取率和辐射效率，但统计分析显示Kerr黑洞对观测数据拟合更佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索Kerr-Sen黑洞在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-伸缩子-轴子（Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton-axion, EMDA）理论框架下的无力磁层特性，特别是伸缩子参数对能量提取过程的影响。

Method: 采用微扰方法求解非线性Grad-Shafranov（GS）方程，确定磁场构型，并量化伸缩子参数r₂对能量提取率和辐射效率的影响；同时使用χ²统计分析方法处理六个黑洞双星系统的观测数据。

Result: 结果显示能量提取功率和辐射效率均随伸缩子参数r₂增加而提升，超过标准Kerr黑洞；但提取效率与Kerr情况一致。统计分析表明，对于洛伦兹因子Γ=2和5的情况，Kerr黑洞对观测数据拟合更好。

Conclusion: Kerr-Sen黑洞的伸缩子参数能增强能量提取过程，但当前观测数据更支持标准Kerr黑洞模型，这为黑洞磁层理论和观测约束提供了新见解。

Abstract: We investigate the steady, axisymmetric, force-free magnetosphere of Kerr-Sen black hole (BH) within the framework of the Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton-axion (EMDA) theory. By perturbatively solving the nonlinear Grad-Shafranov (GS) equation, we determine the magnetic field configuration and quantify the influence of the dilaton parameter $r_2$ on the energy extraction rate and radiative efficiency. Our results show that both the energy extraction power and the radiative efficiency increase with $r_2$, exceeding those of the standard Kerr BH, whereas the extraction efficiency remain consistent with the Kerr case. In addition, we perform $χ^2$ statistical analysis using observational data from six binary BH systems, which indicates that the Kerr BH currently provides a better fit for bulk Lorentz factors $Γ= 2$ and $5$.

</details>


### [9] [New symmetry for the imperfect fluid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03397)
*Alcides Garat*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种针对含涡旋（vorticity）非完美流体（imperfect fluid）的四速度规范变换（four-velocity gauge-like transformations）新对称性，并发展了类似爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦时空（Einstein-Maxwell spacetimes）的标架（tetrad）形式体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在探索非完美流体在存在涡旋时的新对称性，通过引入局部四速度规范变换来建立类似电磁规范不变性的流体动力学对称性框架。

Method: 采用类似先前手稿中爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦时空形式体系的标架（tetrad）表述，为不完美流体发展相应的数学框架。引入局部四速度规范变换，并研究应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensor）在此变换下的不变性条件。

Result: 四速度旋度（four-velocity curl）和度规张量（metric tensor）在四速度规范变换下保持不变。通过引入应力-能量张量中多个变量的附加变换，可使非完美流体应力-能量张量在局部四速度规范变换下保持不变。特别构建了在局部四速度规范变换下不变的涡旋应力-能量张量（vorticity stress-energy tensor）。

Conclusion: 该理论框架为含涡旋非完美流体提供了新的对称性描述，通过中子星（neutron stars）应用展示了新标架体系带来的简化优势，为流体动力学对称性研究开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We will address the existence of a new symmetry for an imperfect fluid by introducing local four-velocity gauge-like transformations for the case when there is vorticity. A similar tetrad formulation as to the Einstein-Maxwell spacetimes formalism presented in previous manuscripts will be developed in this manuscript for the imperfect fluids. The four-velocity curl and the metric tensor will be invariant under these kind of four-velocity gauge-like local transformations. While the Einstein-Maxwell stress-energy tensor is locally gauge invariant under electromagnetic gauge transformations, the perfect fluid stress-energy tensor will not be invariant under four-velocity gauge-like local transformations. We will dedicate our analysis to the imperfect fluid stress-energy tensor that will be invariant under local four-velocity gauge-like transformations when additional transformations are introduced for several variables included in the stress-energy tensor itself. We will also pay special attention to the construction of a vorticity stress-energy tensor invariant under local four-velocity gauge-like transformations. An application on neutron stars will be developed in order to show the simplifications brought about by these new tetrads.

### [10] [Lower-dimensional Gauss-Bonnet gravity black holes with quintessence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03408)
*G. Alencar,T. M. Crispim,J. Macedo,C. R. Muniz*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索精质物质对低维引力理论和黑洞性质的深刻影响，特别是在高斯-博内引力扩展框架下，为理解低维引力理论和黑洞最终状态提供新视角。

Method: 采用$D\to3$极限下的高斯-博内引力与精质物质耦合的理论框架，通过求解场方程获得精确解，并进行了测地线分析和热力学稳定性研究。

Result: 获得了扩展BTZ度规的精确解，发现事件视界半径随精质参数$ω_q$增大而减小，且存在曲率奇点；测地线分析显示稳定圆形光子轨道仅存在于幻影型精质（$ω_q < -1$）情况；热力学上系统稳定，蒸发后形成稳定残余物。

Conclusion: 精质物质对(2+1)维黑洞的几何和热力学性质具有深刻影响，所有物理量都内在依赖于高斯-博内扩展参数$α$，这为低维引力理论和黑洞最终状态研究提供了新视角。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the $D\to3$ limit of Gauss-Bonnet gravity with quintessential matter, obtaining exact solutions that extend the BTZ metric through higher-curvature terms and quintessence coupling. The solutions exhibit a single event horizon whose radius decreases with increasing quintessence parameter $ω_q$, while developing a curvature singularity at the origin for non-vanishing quintessence. The geodesic analysis reveals stable circular photon orbits exist exclusively for phantom-like quintessence ($ω_q < -1$). Thermodynamically, the system is stable, since the specific heat is positive, and with evaporation it evolves to stable remnants whose characteristic size decreases as $ω_q$ increases, with complete evaporation prevented by quintessence effects. Furthermore, we find that all physical quantities intrinsically depend on the parameter $α$ of the Gauss-Bonnet extension.These results demonstrate the profound influence of quintessential matter on both geometric and thermodynamic properties of (2+1)-dimensional black holes, offering new perspectives on gravitational theories in lower dimensions and black hole final states.

### [11] [Lower bound on the radii of black-hole shadows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03421)
*Shahar Hod*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明了在满足弱能量条件（weak energy condition）的球对称有毛黑洞时空中，黑洞阴影半径存在下界：$r_{\text{sh}}/r_{\text{H}}\geq 3\sqrt{3}/2$，其中史瓦西黑洞的阴影恰好达到该下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性耦合的爱因斯坦-物质场方程预测了黑洞周围存在具有明确边界的阴影。研究旨在探索在球对称有毛黑洞时空中，这些阴影半径是否存在普遍的下界约束。

Method: 采用解析证明方法，在球对称有毛黑洞时空框架下，要求物质场满足弱能量条件（weak energy condition），推导阴影半径与视界半径之间的无量纲关系。

Result: 证明了阴影半径存在严格下界：$r_{\text{sh}}/r_{\text{H}}\geq 3\sqrt{3}/2$，其中史瓦西黑洞（bald Schwarzschild black hole）的阴影特征恰好达到该解析下界。

Conclusion: 在满足弱能量条件的球对称有毛黑洞时空中，黑洞阴影半径存在普遍的下界约束，该约束与史瓦西黑洞的阴影半径一致，为黑洞阴影观测提供了理论基准。

Abstract: The non-linearly coupled Einstein-matter field equations predict the existence of shadows with well-defined boundaries around black holes. We prove that, in spherically symmetric hairy black-hole spacetimes whose matter fields satisfy the weak energy condition, the radii of these shadows are bounded from below by the dimensionless relation $r_{\text{sh}}/r_{\text{H}}\geq 3\sqrt{3}/2$, where $r_{\text{H}}$ is the horizon radius of the central hairy black hole. The characteristic shadow of the (bald) Schwarzschild black-hole spacetime saturates the analytically derived lower bound.

### [12] [The effects of non Bunch-Davies initial conditions on gravitationally produced relics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03430)
*Enrico Bertuzzo,Gabriel M. Salla,Andrea Tesi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了非Bunch-Davies初始条件对宇宙学遗迹粒子丰度的影响，特别关注能够再现暗物质总丰度的参数空间。研究发现，对于仅通过质量项破坏共形对称性的粒子，初始条件选择对暗物质相关质量范围影响较小；而对于其他粒子（如自旋1的纵向模式），则与标准计算存在显著偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统引力产生遗迹粒子的研究通常假设Bunch-Davies初始条件（即初始真空无粒子态）。本文旨在探究非Bunch-Davies初始条件对最终遗迹粒子丰度的影响，特别关注能够再现暗物质总丰度的参数空间。

Method: 提出了适用于任何初始条件的通用框架，通过该框架分析初始条件对谱函数和晚期丰度的非平凡影响。研究特别考察了初始热态和两阶段暴胀情景，以具体示例和量化结果说明初始条件的影响。

Result: 对于仅通过质量项破坏共形对称性（conformal symmetry breaking）的粒子（如自旋1/2费米子和共形耦合标量场），初始条件选择对暗物质相关质量范围影响较小。然而，对于其他粒子（如自旋1的纵向模式），观测到与标准计算存在显著偏差。通过初始热态和两阶段暴胀情景的量化分析表明，暗物质总丰度可在广泛的质量范围内获得。

Conclusion: 非Bunch-Davies初始条件对遗迹粒子丰度具有重要影响，特别是对于某些粒子类型。研究强调了初始条件选择在暗物质产生机制中的关键作用，并表明暗物质总丰度可在广泛的质量参数范围内通过适当的初始条件实现。

Abstract: Typical gravitational production of relics from amplification of inflationary perturbations assumes Bunch-Davies initial conditions, i.e. a vacuum with initially no particles. In this paper we investigate the impact of non Bunch-Davies initial conditions to the final abundance of relics, with particular attention to the parameter space where the total dark matter abundance is reproduced. We present a general framework for any initial condition, through which we show their non-trivial effect on both spectrum and late-time abundance. We argue that for particles whose source of conformal symmetry breaking comes only from a mass term (spin-1/2 fermions and conformally coupled scalars), the choice of initial conditions has little impact on the mass range relevant to dark matter. For other particles, e.g. the longitudinal mode of spin-1, we see a large deviation from the standard computation. We exemplify and quantify our results with an initial thermal state and a two-stage inflation scenario, highlighting that the total dark matter can be obtained for a wide range of masses.

Result: 膜上的有效宇宙学常数$\Lambda(y)$作为额外维度的函数自然涌现，并被体空间的弯曲几何所生成和束缚；模型无需在膜上引入基本宇宙学常数即可再现加速膨胀解，表明宇宙加速源于膜的嵌入和体空间的引力动力学。

Abstract: This work investigates the cosmology of a thick brane within the context of $f(\mathbb{Q})$ gravity, an extension of symmetric teleparallelism. Using a five-dimensional Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker metric, we solve the field equations to obtain dynamic solutions for the scale factor. We demonstrate that the effective cosmological constant on the brane naturally emerges as a function of the extra dimension $Λ(y)$, being both generated and confined by the curved geometry of the bulk. We analyze two distinct regimes: Randall-Sundrum-type thin brane and thick brane through the Sine-Gordon model. Our model reproduces accelerated expansion solutions without requiring the introduction of a fundamental cosmological constant on the brane, showing that the cosmic acceleration emerges as a consequence of the brane's embedding and the gravitational dynamics in the bulk . The variation of the $c_i$ parameters in symmetric teleparallelism enables different cosmological scenarios, including de Sitter-type expansion, contraction, and oscillatory solutions. The results indicate that the brane's position in the bulk determines its cosmology, providing a geometric explanation for the smallness of the observed cosmological constant.

Method: 采用标量、矢量和纯张量分解（decomposition in terms of scalar, vectorial, and purely tensorial objects）分析方程结构，并实施微扰方法（perturbative approach）研究带电非旋转BTZ（BTZ charged, non-rotating metric）背景解附近的修正。

Abstract: We consider a metric-affine formulation of Chern-Simons modified gravity in 2 + 1 dimensions. The theory is built requiring projective invariance, and the structure of the equations is analyzed using a decomposition in terms of scalar, vectorial, and purely tensorial objects. This approach allows us to implement a perturbative approach to study the corrections that emerge around a given background solution, for which we consider a BTZ charged, non-rotating metric. We show that conditions on model parameters are necessary to keep perturbations under control, yielding a rotating solution with a constant angular momentum and magnetic field at the horizon, and a smooth decay further away. We comment on the possibility of going beyond the leading order in perturbations and on its dynamical implications.

### [15] [Accelerating Bertotti-Robinson Black Holes in a Uniform Magnetic Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03494)

Abstract: We study the Hawking temperature, geodesic motion, and observable signatures of the accelerating Bertotti-Robinson (BR) spacetime, a vacuum black-hole solution deformed by a uniform magnetic field $B$ and an acceleration parameter $α$. In the timelike sector, we derive the effective potential for massive particles, determine the specific energy and angular momentum for equatorial circular orbits, and determine how $(B,α)$ shifts the ISCO; we also illustrate representative trajectories of massive particles. ### [17] [The Maxwell-Higgs System with Scalar Potential on Subextremal Kerr Spacetimes: Nonlinear wave operators and asymptotic completeness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04202)
*Bobby Eka Gunara,Mulyanto,Fiki Taufik Akbar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文在四维亚极端克尔黑洞的外通讯区域上，为满足特定条件的麦克斯韦-希格斯系统构造了非线性波算符，并证明了小数据渐近完备性，建立了规范不变的散射映射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究亚极端克尔黑洞背景下麦克斯韦-希格斯系统的非线性散射理论，特别是在辐射（无电荷）区域中建立规范不变的散射映射，处理规范协变辐射场描述的渐近态。

Method: 采用从非齐次克莱因-戈登场和无电荷麦克斯韦场的线性估计包到非线性系统的转移原理（transfer principle），在无质量克尔情况下验证了线性估计包，并在史瓦西时空中独立证明了该估计包。

Result: 构造了非线性波算符并证明了小数据渐近完备性，建立了规范不变的散射映射，该映射是小数据的双射，在0处弗雷歇可微且导数等于线性克尔散射，具有二次（玻恩）展开和O(‖U‖³)余项。

Conclusion: 在亚极端克尔黑洞背景下成功建立了麦克斯韦-希格斯系统的非线性散射理论，散射映射在自然渐近拓扑中具有良好性质，对于解析的标量势P是实解析的，无质量情况在整个亚极端范围内无条件成立。

Abstract: We construct nonlinear wave operators and prove small-data asymptotic completeness for the Maxwell--Higgs system on the domain of outer communications of every four-dimensional subextremal Kerr black hole $(\mathcal D_{M,a},g_{M,a})$ with $M>0$ and $|a|<M$, for gauge-invariant nonnegative scalar potentials $P$ satisfying Assumption~\ref{asumsiP} with mass parameter $m^{2}\ge0$. The massless case $m=0$ is unconditional on the full subextremal range. For $m^{2}>0$ the same conclusions follow assuming the massive linear package $\Lin_{k}^{(m)}$ for the linear comparison system (in particular, no exponentially growing modes); this fails for an open set of masses due to superradiant instability \cite{ShlapentokhRothmanKGKerr}. We work in the radiative (charge-free) regime; stationary Coulomb (Kerr--Newman) modes are treated separately. Asymptotic states are described by gauge-covariant radiation fields on $\mathcal I^{\pm}\cup\mathcal H^{\pm}$ (and, when $m>0$, an additional timelike/Dollard channel), yielding a gauge-invariant nonlinear scattering map on the residual-gauge quotient. The scattering map is a small-data bijection, is Fréchet differentiable at $0$ with derivative equal to linear Kerr scattering, admits a quadratic (Born) expansion with an $O(\|U\|^{3})$ remainder in the natural asymptotic topology, and is real-analytic for analytic $P$. The nonlinear argument is presented as a transfer principle from a black-box linear estimate package for inhomogeneous Klein--Gordon and charge-free Maxwell fields, verified here in the massless Kerr case (and proved self-contained in Schwarzschild).

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立扩展不确定性原理（Extended Uncertainty Principle, EUP）与时空度规之间的直接对应关系，探索EUP对黑洞热力学性质和光学特征的影响，特别是光子球半径和阴影尺寸的变化规律。

Abstract: An explicit correspondence is established between the Extended Uncertainty Principle (EUP) and the metric function by directly relating the radiation temperature function modified by EUP to the modified spacetime metric. Utilising this modified metric, we subsequently derive the corresponding thermodynamic quantities of the black hole, and calculate the photon sphere radius and the size of the black hole shadow. The results of the study indicate that, in comparison with Schwarzschild black holes, the position of the event horizon remains constant under EUP modifications. However, the photon sphere radius increases with growing EUP parameters, while the shadow size decreases with increasing parameters, demonstrating that EUP induces optical shift phenomena. By comparing with observations of the galactic centre black hole $\text{Sgr}{\text{A}^{*}}$ from the Event Horizon Telescope, new constraints are established on EUP parameters.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索通过黑洞准正规模（quasinormal modes）探测强引力区域宇称破坏（parity-violating）物理的新途径。宇称破坏效应通过保角变换因子编码在黑洞解中，为研究非标准引力理论提供了理想平台。

Method: 采用微扰方法，在保角Kerr（conformal Kerr）背景下研究最小耦合到引力的测试标量场的准正规模。对宇称破坏效应进行微扰处理，同时允许黑洞自旋从非旋转情况到近极端（near-extremal）区域的任意取值。

Abstract: Recently, an exact rotating black hole solution in a parity-violating theory of gravity was obtained via a conformal transformation of the Kerr solution in general relativity, with parity-violating effects encoded in the conformal factor. We study the quasinormal modes (QNMs) of a test scalar field minimally coupled to gravity on this conformal Kerr background, treating the parity-violating effects perturbatively while allowing for arbitrary black hole spin, from the non-rotating case to the near-extremal regime. For low spin, we derive a perturbative formula for the QNM frequencies that includes the leading-order parity-violating correction. For high spin, particularly in the near-extremal regime, we find sizable deviations from the Kerr QNM frequencies. Our results point to a new avenue for probing parity-violating physics in the strong-gravity regime through black hole QNMs.

Method: 构建了适应于测地线观测者的局部惯性参考系（locally inertial reference system），并引入径向锁定参考系（radially locked reference system）确保空间方向一致性；通过计算尘埃测地线之间交换光子的频率偏移（frequency shift）来分析尘埃构型。

Abstract: In this work, we construct a locally inertial reference system adapted to a geodesic observer in stationary, axisymmetric dust solutions of the Einstein equations employed as effective models of a portion of a galactic disc. To ensure a consistent spatial orientation among different local observers, we also introduce the radially locked reference system, in which one spatial axis is aligned with the radial direction defined by null geodesics passing through the galactic center. Within this framework, we analyze how the dust configuration is described by such observers by computing the frequency shift of photons exchanged between pairs of dust geodesics. Building on this construction, we outline a procedure to reconstruct spectroscopic and astrometric relative velocities with respect to locally inertial observers, providing a coherent foundation for the study of galactic kinematics in a fully general relativistic context.

### [21] [Lorentzian-Euclidean singularity-free solutions to gravitational collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03934)
*Sune Rastad Bahn,Michael Cramer Andersen*

TL;DR: 该研究探索了静态球对称爱因斯坦方程的奇点自由解，以标准史瓦西解为边界条件。通过消除曲率奇点并要求度规时间分量的可微性，发现解在视界处出现符号变化，导致局部等效原理违反。研究找到了视界内的"宇宙学常数"型解，并重新发现了完美流体模型中的相同几何结构。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法基于静态球对称爱因斯坦方程，施加两个关键条件：消除曲率奇点（curvature singularities）和要求度规时间分量的可微性（differentiability）。研究采用标准史瓦西解作为边界条件，并考虑不可压缩完美流体（incompressible perfect fluid）服从托尔曼-奥本海默-沃尔科夫方程（Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equation）的恒星残骸模型。

Result: 研究发现视界内存在一个简单的"宇宙学常数"型应力-能量张量（"cosmological constant" stress-energy tensor）解。对于完美流体模型，重新发现了相同的几何结构，表明该模型在数学和物理上都具有可行性。研究还发现了一个新的理论极限M/R=3/8，低于布赫达尔极限（Buchdahl limit）的M/R=4/9，该极限描述了完美流体密度将退回到事件视界之后的条件。

Conclusion: 研究讨论了状态方程（equation of state），并提出最终状态可由希格斯样自由标量场（Higgs-like free scalar field）描述。该模型在视界处度规符号变化导致局部等效原理违反，但数学和物理上仍然可行，为奇点自由解提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: This study explores singularity-free solutions to the static, spherical symmetric Einstein equations with the standard Schwarzschild solution as a boundary condition. Imposing the absence of curvature singularities and requiring differentiability of the time component of the metric leads to a sign change across the horizon, violating the Principle of Equivalence locally. We find a solution within the event horizon with a simple ``cosmological constant'' stress-energy tensor. Considering the impact of sign change to a compact stellar remnant, modeled by an incompressible perfect fluid obeying the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equation, we rediscover the same geometry, indicating both mathematical and physical feasibility of the model. We also find a new theoretical limit M/R=3/8, which is lower than the Buchdahl limit of M/R=4/9 for the density of a perfect fluid that will recede behind an event horizon. The equation of state is discussed, and we propose that the final state is described by a Higgs-like free scalar field.

Due to the form of this phenomenological energy density ansatz, which starts to rise with the nonlinear structure growth in the universe and falls with the domination of cosmic voids, we prefer to call it structure-induced dark energy. Abstract: We develop a systematic framework for formulating and solving the conditions that lead to separability in stationary, axisymmetric spacetimes in the presence of matter fields. Guided by Carter's metric form, we introduce a general stationary, axisymmetric metric ansatz that allows for a transparent separation of radial and angular variables. This construction yields a broad family of stationary rotating solutions admitting separability structures. To illustrate the applicability of the formalism, we explicitly construct several examples, including a rotating black hole with a global monopole supported by anisotropic matter, as well as a new class of rotating wormhole geometries.

### [24] [Non-minimally coupled loop quantum inflation with inverse-volume corrections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04182)
*Rudranil Roy,Giovanni Otalora,Joel Saavedra,Salvatore Capozziello*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了在包含逆体积修正的圈量子宇宙学（LQC）有效框架下，由非最小耦合标量场驱动的慢滚暴胀。通过分析两类势能函数并推导暴胀可观测量，发现模型符合当前观测约束，且非最小耦合参数ξ显著增加了有利初始条件的相空间体积。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探讨圈量子宇宙学（Loop Quantum Cosmology, LQC）有效框架下，包含逆体积修正的非最小耦合标量场驱动的慢滚暴胀（slow-roll inflation）。特别关注两类物理动机明确的势能函数：类希格斯四次势和受弦理论启发的分数幂次单项式势。

Method: 方法包括在慢滚展开的一阶近似下，推导暴胀可观测量（标量谱指数n_s、张标比r、跑动α_s）的解析表达式。通过数值求解修正的背景动力学获得定量预测，并使用有效相空间上的正则刘维尔测度（canonical Liouville measure）计算获得足够长暴胀相的概率。

Conclusion: 结论表明在LQC框架下，非最小耦合标量场暴胀模型与当前观测数据兼容。尽管有效LQC用量子反弹取代初始奇点，但获得足够长暴胀相的概率依赖于暴胀前动力学和暴胀子势能，其中非最小耦合参数ξ对有利初始条件有显著增强作用。

Abstract: We study slow-roll inflation driven by a scalar field non-minimally coupled to gravity within the effective framework of Loop Quantum Cosmology (LQC), including inverse-volume corrections. We consider two physically motivated classes of potentials, a Higgs-like quartic potential $V\proptoφ^{4}$ and string-inspired fractional monomial potentials $V\proptoφ^{p}$ with $p<1$. Working at first order in the slow-roll expansion, we derive analytic expressions for the inflationary observables, namely the scalar spectral index $n_s$, the tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$, and the running $α_s\equiv dn_s/d\ln k$, and then solve the corrected background dynamics numerically to obtain quantitative predictions. Confronting these results with current observational constraints from Planck 2018 and ACT DR6, we find that the model can lie within the allowed region of the $(n_s,r,α_s)$ parameter space, including a mild preference for slightly larger $n_s$, as suggested by recent ground-based measurements. We also compute the probability of achieving sufficient slow-roll inflation in this setting. Although effective LQC replaces the initial singularity with a nonsingular quantum bounce, the likelihood of a sufficiently long inflationary phase depends on the pre-inflationary dynamics and on the inflaton potential. Using the canonical Liouville measure on the effective phase space, we determine the fraction of post-bounce trajectories that yield sufficient inflation and find that the non-minimal coupling parameter $ξ$ substantially enlarges the phase-space volume of favorable initial conditions relative to the minimally coupled case, exhibiting an attractor-like enhancement that saturates at large $ξ$.

### [25] [Non-Hermitian Quantum Mechanics with Applications to Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04375)
*Oem Trivedi,Alfredo Gurrola,Robert J. Scherrer*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出厄米性（Hermiticity）并非量子力学的基本公理，而是内积流（inner product current）全局守恒产生的对称性定律。在黑洞视界等因果视界存在时，这种守恒被破坏，导致有效非厄米生成元（non-Hermitian generator）的出现，并与广义第二定律（generalized second law）和爱因斯坦方程（Einstein equations）的结构相统一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上厄米性被视为量子力学的基本公理，保证实数谱和幺正时间演化。本文旨在重新理解厄米性的本质，探讨其在存在因果视界（causal horizons）的时空中的表现，特别是黑洞几何中的情况。

Method: 通过分析时空中的内积流守恒，在存在完整柯西曲面（complete Cauchy surfaces）的情况下推导出标准厄米条件。在因果视界存在时，利用量子热力学（quantum thermodynamics）和相对熵单调性（monotonicity of relative entropy），将广义第二定律重新解释为熵平衡。结合爱因斯坦方程的比安基恒等式（Bianchi identity）和Raychaudhuri聚焦方程（Raychaudhuri focusing equation）提供几何机制。

Result: 证明在因果视界存在时，内积流守恒被破坏，导致完全正迹保持动力学（completely positive trace preserving dynamics）和有效非厄米生成元。广义第二定律可精确补偿通过视界的内积荷通量（inner product charge flux）。黑洞环降（black hole ringdown）可作为观测探针，提供视界诱导内积流通量的定量上限。

Conclusion: 重力、熵产生和有效非厄米性在单一结构原理下统一，厄米性仅作为内积对称性全局守恒的特殊情况出现。这一框架将量子力学基本对称性与时空几何和热力学定律联系起来。

Abstract: Hermiticity is usually treated as a foundational axiom of quantum mechanics, guaranteeing real spectra and unitary time evolution. In this work we argue that Hermiticity is more naturally understood as a symmetry law arising from the global conservation of an inner product current. We show that in spacetimes admitting complete Cauchy surfaces without boundary flux this conservation reduces to the familiar Hermiticity condition of the canonical inner product. However, in the presence of causal horizons, most strikingly in black hole geometries, this conservation law becomes obstructed for restricted observers. Tracing over inaccessible degrees of freedom then inevitably yields completely positive trace preserving dynamics with an effective non-Hermitian generator. Using quantum thermodynamics and the monotonicity of relative entropy, we demonstrate that the generalized second law may be reinterpreted as an entropy balance that compensates precisely for the flux of inner product charge through the horizon. The structure of Einstein equations, through the Bianchi identity and the Raychaudhuri focusing equation, provides the geometric mechanism underlying this balance. We also show that black hole ringdown can serve as a realistic observational probe of this idea and may provide quantitative upper bounds on the strength of horizon-induced inner product flux. In this way gravity, entropy production, and effective non-Hermiticity are unified under a single structural principle, with Hermiticity emerging as the special case of globally conserved inner product symmetry.

</details>


### [26] [Gravitational confinement of ghost scalar fields in neutron stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04400)
*Argelia Bernal,Víctor Jaramillo,Néstor A. Montiel-Hernández,Darío Núñez,Nicolas Sanchis-Gual*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了具有负动能项的幽灵标量物质（ghost scalar matter）在中子星核心内的效应、稳定性及非线性动力学，发现中子星能够引力束缚有限量的幽灵物质并支持连续平衡解族，且系统表现出持续的脉冲状振荡运动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索具有负动能项的幽灵标量物质模型在中子星核心内的物理效应，特别是其稳定性与非线性动力学行为，以理解这类奇异物质形态在天体物理环境中的表现。

Method: 研究方法包括分析耦合的爱因斯坦-欧拉-(幽灵，复)克莱因-戈登系统（Einstein-Euler-(ghost, complex) Klein-Gordon system）的静态构型，并对代表性案例进行完全动力学的数值演化计算。

Result: 研究结果表明中子星能够引力束缚有限量的幽灵物质并支持连续平衡解族，表明这些构型并非精细调谐的结果。中子星经历持续的脉冲状振荡运动，且恒星流体振荡模式与幽灵标量场模式之间存在频率同步现象。

Conclusion: 该研究证实了幽灵标量物质在中子星核心内的可束缚性及其动力学稳定性，揭示了系统振荡模式间的频率同步机制，为理解奇异物质在天体物理环境中的行为提供了新见解。

Abstract: We investigate the effects, stability, and nonlinear dynamics of ghost scalar matter modeled as a field with a negative kinetic term confined within the cores of neutron stars. To this end, we analyze static configurations of the coupled Einstein-Euler-(ghost, complex) Klein-Gordon system and then we perform fully dynamical numerical evolutions of illustrative cases. Our results demonstrate that neutron stars can gravitationally confine a finite amount of ghost matter and support continuous families of equilibrium solutions, indicating that these configurations are not the result of fine tuning. We analyze the properties of the final states and find that the neutron star undergoes a persistent pulse-like oscillatory motion. In particular, we explicitly compute the frequency synchronization between the stellar fluid oscillation modes and those of the ghost scalar sector.

</details>

### [27] [Enhancing Angular Sensitivity of Segmented Antineutrino Detectors for Reactor Monitoring Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03561)
*Brian C. Crow,Max A. A. Dornfest,John G. Learned,Jackson D. Seligman,Nathan S. Sibert,Jeffrey G. Yepez,Viacheslav A. Li*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种改进的反β衰变探测器（inverse-beta-decay detectors）中反中微子方向性（antineutrino directionality）确定方法，通过基于矩阵间"距离"度量的新算法，解决了传统方法在整体式和分段式探测器（monolithic and segmented detectors）中的模糊性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统用于量化整体式和分段式探测器方向性的方法存在方法论上的模糊性。本文旨在改进反β衰变探测器中反中微子方向性确定的标准方法，特别是在低计数区域（low-count regime）的应用场景。

Method: 开发了一种基于两个矩阵间"距离"度量的新方向性算法，并将探测器分段数据以矩阵形式处理。算法验证通过比较蒙特卡洛生成的"经验"数据集（Monte Carlo generated empirical data set）与模拟数据集完成，其中经验数据集针对特定中微子束方向生成。

Result: 确定了低计数区域中的最优分段尺度（optimal segmentation scale）。算法在计算效率高的二维模式匹配（computationally efficient 2D pattern-matching）方面具有广泛应用潜力，特别是在反应堆反中微子方向性研究中。

Conclusion: 新算法不仅改进了传统方法的不足，其应用可扩展到分段探测器、混合设计（hybrid designs）和广义验证，且与探测器设计的物理原理无关（agnostic to the physics of detector design）。

Abstract: We present a potential improvement over the standard method developed to determine antineutrino directionality in inverse-beta-decay detectors. The previously developed method for quantifying directionality in monolithic and segmented detectors may be ambiguous in methodology. In this paper, we present a new directionality algorithm and include error analysis. We have developed a new algorithm based on a measure of ``distance'' between two matrices. We report findings for our research in reactor-antineutrino directionality, and emphasize that the algorithm has broad applications whenever one desires computationally efficient 2D pattern-matching. We treat data from detector segments in the form of a matrix. The validation of our algorithm boils down to comparing a Monte Carlo generated ``empirical'' data set to a simulated data set. The empirical data set is generated for a particular orientation of the neutrino beam. We identify an optimal segmentation scale in the low-count regime. We also discuss the shortcomings of the conventional method and how this knowledge can be applied to segmented detectors, hybrid designs, and generalized validation, agnostic to the physics of detector design.

</details>


### [28] [Measurement of angular correlations inside jets induced by gluon polarization in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13.6 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03689)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究利用CMS探测器在13.6 TeV质子-质子对撞中测量了喷注内部角关联，开发了识别喷注子结构特征的新技术，发现结果支持包含胶子极化效应的模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究胶子极化（gluon polarization）在部分子簇射（parton shower）中对喷注内部角关联的影响，以验证量子色动力学（QCD）中胶子自旋效应的理论预测。

Method: 采用CMS探测器收集的34.7 fb⁻¹积分亮度数据，使用anti-kₜ算法重建喷注，随后用Cambridge-Aachen算法进行解聚类（declustering），开发了识别喷注子结构特征和选择中间胶子分裂为夸克-反夸克对的新分析技术。

Result: 测量了对胶子极化敏感的观测量，并与PYTHIA 8和HERWIG 7模型预测进行比较，结果与包含胶子极化效应的模型一致，强烈排斥忽略胶子极化的模型。

Conclusion: 研究证实了胶子极化在部分子簇射中产生角关联的重要性，为理解量子色动力学的非微扰效应提供了实验证据，支持包含胶子自旋效应的理论框架。

Abstract: A study of angular correlations inside jets induced by gluon polarization is performed using proton-proton collisions at a center-of-mass energy of $\sqrt{s}$ = 13.6 TeV. The data correspond to an integrated luminosity of 34.7 fb$^{-1}$, collected in 2022 with the CMS detector at the LHC. The details of the parton shower are investigated using jets reconstructed with the anti-$k_\mathrm{T}$ algorithm and subsequently declustered with the Cambridge$-$Aachen algorithm. A novel analysis technique is developed to identify characteristic features of the jet substructure and to select intermediate gluon splittings into quark-antiquark pairs. An observable sensitive to gluon polarization in the parton shower is measured and compared with PYTHIA 8 and HERWIG 7 model predictions, with and without angular correlations induced by the gluon spin. The results are consistent with models that incorporate gluon polarization and strongly disfavor those that neglect them.

</details>


### [29] [Imaging baryon number density within the proton](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03730)
*Spencer R. Klein,Mathias C. Labonte,Zachary Sweger,Gerald A. Miller,Ramona Vogt*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析光子-质子碰撞产生的四个介子产生通道，首次测量了质子内重子数（baryon number）的横向空间分布，发现重子数集中在质子中心约0.33-0.53 fm范围内，显著小于电荷和质量分布半径（≥0.67 fm）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质子空间结构是核物理的关键参数，不同测量技术探测不同特性（如电荷半径、质量半径、机械半径）。本研究旨在探索质子内重子数（baryon number）这一新特征的空间分布，以更全面理解质子内部结构。

Method: 通过分析光子-质子碰撞（γp）产生的四个专属介子产生通道（p ρ⁰、p ω、n π⁺、p π⁰），提取介子产生截面的横向动量（p_T）依赖性，并利用傅里叶-贝塞尔变换（Fourier-Bessel transformations）推导相互作用系统的二维横向尺寸。

Result: 研究发现重子数被限制在横向半径0.33-0.53 fm范围内，而质子电荷和质量分布的横向半径至少为0.67 fm。这表明重子数集中在质子中心区域，空间分布比电荷和质量更紧凑。

Conclusion: 重子数在质子内部的空间分布特征与电荷和质量分布显著不同，呈现更小的空间范围和中心集中特性。这一发现为理解质子内部结构提供了新的维度，揭示了不同物理量在质子内的空间分布差异。

Abstract: The spatial extent of the proton is a key factor in nuclear physics. Different measurement techniques probe different aspects of the proton, yielding different radii. The mass and charge radii depend on the parton and quark distributions respectively, while the mechanical radius depends on the mass/energy distribution. Here, we probe the spatial distribution of a new proton characteristic, studying the distribution of baryon number within the proton.
  We investigate the baryon number distribution by studying four exclusive meson production channels arising from photon-proton collisions ($γp \rightarrow p ρ^0$, $γp \rightarrow p ω$, $γp \rightarrow n π^+$, and $γp \rightarrow p π^0$). The two-dimensional transverse sizes of the interacting systems are extracted by analyzing the transverse momentum, $p_T$, dependence of the meson production cross section, using Fourier-Bessel transformations. We find that baryon number is confined to a transverse radius of $0.33 - 0.53$~fm. In comparison, the transverse radius of the proton charge and mass distributions are considerably larger, at least 0.67~fm. The baryon number is concentrated in the center of the proton.

</details>


### [30] [End-to-end event reconstruction for precision physics at future colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04084)
*Dolores Garcia,Lena Herrmann,Gregor Krzmanc,Michele Selvaggi*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种端到端的全局事件重建方法，通过几何代数变换器网络和基于对象凝聚的聚类，将带电粒子径迹与量能器、μ子击中直接映射到粒子级对象，在FCC-ee对撞实验中显著提升了重建效率和分辨率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 未来对撞机实验对希格斯（Higgs）、电弱和味观测量测量精度提出了前所未有的要求，这给事件重建带来了严格挑战。当前粒子流算法依赖于探测器特定的聚类，限制了探测器设计阶段的灵活性。

Method: 该方法采用端到端的全局事件重建框架，结合几何代数变换器网络（geometric algebra transformer networks）与基于对象凝聚（object condensation）的聚类，随后使用专用网络进行粒子识别和能量回归（energy regression）。

Result: 在基于CLD探测器概念的FCC-ee电子-正电子对撞全模拟中，该方法相比最先进的基于规则的算法，相对重建效率提升10-20%，带电强子的假粒子率降低达两个数量级，可见能量和不变质量分辨率提升22%。

Conclusion: 该框架通过将重建性能与探测器特定调优解耦，能够在未来对撞机实验的探测器设计阶段实现快速迭代，为高精度测量提供了更灵活高效的重建方案。

Abstract: Future collider experiments require unprecedented precision in measurements of Higgs, electroweak, and flavour observables, placing stringent demands on event reconstruction. The achievable precision on Higgs couplings scales directly with the resolution on visible final state particles and their invariant masses. Current particle flow algorithms rely on detector specific clustering, limiting flexibility during detector design. Here we present an end-to-end global event reconstruction approach that maps charged particle tracks and calorimeter and muon hits directly to particle level objects. The method combines geometric algebra transformer networks with object condensation based clustering, followed by dedicated networks for particle identification and energy regression. Our approach is benchmarked on fully simulated electron positron collisions at FCC-ee using the CLD detector concept. It outperforms the state-of-the-art rule-based algorithm by 10--20\% in relative reconstruction efficiency, achieves up to two orders of magnitude reduction in fake-particle rates for charged hadrons, and improves visible energy and invariant mass resolution by 22\%. By decoupling reconstruction performance from detector-specific tuning, this framework enables rapid iteration during the detector design phase of future collider experiments.

</details>

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: BESIII合作组基于20.3 fb⁻¹数据首次观测到D⁰→K₂*(1430)⁻ℓ⁺νℓ衰变的D波分量（8.0σ显著性），并精确测量了主导的K*(892)⁻分支比和形状因子参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究D⁰→K̄⁰π⁻ℓ⁺νℓ半轻子衰变的衰变动力学，旨在探索其中的不同角动量分量，特别是首次寻找并确认D波分量的存在。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器在BEPCII对撞机上收集的20.3 fb⁻¹正负电子对撞数据（质心能量3.773 GeV），分析D⁰→K̄⁰π⁻ℓ⁺νℓ衰变过程，其中ℓ=e, μ。

Result: 首次观测到D⁰→K₂*(1430)⁻ℓ⁺νℓ衰变的D波分量，统计显著性达8.0σ，占总衰变率的(0.092±0.028stat±0.018syst)%；精确测量了K*(892)⁻分支比和形状因子参数，达到迄今最高精度。

Conclusion: 该研究首次确认了D⁰半轻子衰变中D波分量的存在，提供了最精确的K*(892)⁻分支比和形状因子参数测量，并首次实现了K̄⁰π⁻系统中S波相移的模型无关测量。

Abstract: We report a study of the semileptonic decays $D^0 \rightarrow \bar{K}^0π^-\ell^+ν_{\ell}$ (where $\ell=e,~μ$) based on a sample of $20.3~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ of $e^+e^-$ annihilation data collected at a center-of-mass energy of 3.773~GeV with the BESIII detector at the BEPCII collider. Based on an investigation of the decay dynamics in $D^0 \rightarrow \bar{K}^0π^-\ell^+ν_{\ell}$ decays, a $\mathcal{D}-$wave component of $D^0\rightarrow K_2^*(1430)^-\ell^+ν_{\ell}$ is observed for the first time with a statistical significance of $8.0σ$, in addition to the dominant $K^*(892)^-$ and $\mathcal{S}-$wave components. The $\mathcal{D}-$wave component is determined to account for $(0.092 \pm 0.028_{\rm stat} \pm 0.018_{\rm syst})\%$ of the total decay rate. The branching fractions of the dominant $K^*(892)^-$ components are measured as $\mathcal{B}(D^0\rightarrow K^{*}(892)^-e^+ν_{e}) = (2.043 \pm 0.018_{\rm stat} \pm 0.012_{\rm syst})\%$ and $\mathcal{B}(D^0\rightarrow K^{*}(892)^-μ^+ν_μ) = (1.964 \pm 0.018_{\rm stat} \pm 0.012_{\rm syst})\%$, which are the most precise measurements to date and represent significant improvements over the previous world averages. The hadronic form-factor parameters are measured to be $r_{V} = V(0)/A_1(0) = 1.444 \pm 0.026_{\rm stat} \pm 0.010_{\rm syst}$, $r_{2} = A_2(0)/A_1(0) = 0.752 \pm 0.020_{\rm stat} \pm 0.004_{\rm syst}$, and $A_1(0)=0.618\pm0.002_{\rm stat} \pm0.004_{\rm syst}$, where $V(0)$ is the vector form factor and $A_{1,2}(0)$ are the axial-vector form factors evaluated at $q^2=0$. This is the most precise determination of the form-factor parameters to date measured in a $D\rightarrow K^*(892)$ transition. In addition, we report the first model-independent measurement of the $\mathcal{S}-$wave phase shift in the hadronic $\bar{K}^0π^-$ system.

</details>


### [32] [Experimental Advances on Light Baryon Spectroscopy at BESIII Experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04141)
*Shi Wang,Hao Liu,Shuangshi Fang,Xiongfei Wang*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: BESIII实验利用其在τ-粲物理能区积累的世界最大数据集，在重子谱学研究中取得突破性进展，包括发现多种激发态重子，为理解非微扰QCD和解决"缺失重子共振态"问题提供了关键实验支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BESIII实验作为目前世界上唯一在τ-粲物理能区运行的电子-正电子对撞机，积累了在质心能量1.84-4.95 GeV范围内世界最大的数据集，包括约100亿J/ψ事件和30亿ψ(3686)事件。这些具有高统计量和低本底特性的独特数据集为研究轻重子谱学提供了前所未有的实验条件。

Method: 文章系统回顾了BESIII在重子谱学（baryon spectroscopy）方面的进展，重点关注利用其独特数据集进行的实验研究。该方法基于BESIII在τ-粲物理能区（tau-charm physical energy region）积累的高质量数据，包括近阈值区域的开放粲强子对产生数据。

Result: BESIII取得了突破性成就，包括发现了激发态核子态（excited nucleon states）、Λ超子态（Λ hyperon states）、Σ超子态（Σ hyperon states）、Ξ超子态（Ξ hyperon states）和Ω⁻超子态（Ω⁻ hyperon states）。这些发现扩展了重子激发态的谱系。

Conclusion: BESIII的重子谱学研究结果为理解非微扰QCD（non-perturbative QCD）和解决"缺失重子共振态（missing baryon resonances）"问题提供了关键实验支持。这些进展显著推进了重子谱学领域的研究。

Abstract: The BESIII experiment is currently the world's only electron-positron collider operating in the tau-charm physical energy region. Since starting data taking in 2009, BESIII has accumulated the world's largest data set in the center-of-mass energy range of 1.84-4.95 GeV, including approximately 10 billion $J/ψ$ events and 3 billion $ψ(3686)$ events, together with extensive data on open-charm hadron pair production near threshold regions. These unique datasets, characterized by high statistics and low background, provide unprecedented experimental conditions for studying light baryon spectroscopy. This article systematically reviews the progress made by BESIII in baryon spectroscopy, with a focus on recent breakthrough achievements, including the discovery of excited nucleon states, $Λ$ hyperon states, $Σ$ hyperon states, $Ξ$ hyperon states and $Ω^{-}$ hyperon states. These results expand the spectrum of baryon excited states and provide crucial experimental support for understanding non-perturbative QCD and resolving the ``missing baryon resonances'' problem.

</details>

Result: 论文展示了此类搜索的最新结果，但摘要中未提供具体的发现或排除限度的详细信息。

Conclusion: 摘要未明确给出结论，但暗示了通过CMS实验数据对多种新物理模型预言的重介子进行搜索是可行的，并已获得相关结果。

### [34] [$e^+e^- \rightarrow s\bar{s}$ at $\sqrt{s} = 250$ GeV at future linear colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04200)
*J. P. Márquez,R. Pöeschl,A. Irles,F. Richard*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究评估了未来线性对撞机上正负电子对撞产生奇异夸克对过程中前向-后向不对称性（$A_{FB}$）的测量可行性，重点分析了粒子鉴别技术对电荷重建和不对称性提取的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轻夸克产生过程中的前向-后向不对称性是电弱相互作用（electroweak sector）的灵敏探针，能够探测潜在的味依赖（flavour-dependent）新物理效应（BSM effects）。研究旨在评估未来对撞机实验中进行精确测量的可行性。

Method: 研究采用完整ILD模拟和重建工具，针对ILC和LCF@CERN在质心能量$\sqrt{s}=250$ GeV的正负电子对撞过程$e^+e^- \rightarrow s\bar{s}$。评估了粒子鉴别（PID）对电荷重建和$A_{FB}$提取的影响，考虑了使用综合PID（CPID）优化$dE/dx$的软件改进，以及包含簇计数（$dN/dx$）和理想TPC性能的硬件方案。

Result: 研究结果表明，精确测量$A_{FB}^{s\bar{s}}$是可行的。评估了统计精度的提升，并应用了电荷误识别和接受度的修正。先进的粒子鉴别技术对于最大化对电弱效应和新物理效应的灵敏度至关重要。

Conclusion: 精确的前向-后向不对称性测量在未来线性对撞机上是可行的，先进的粒子鉴别技术是最大化对电弱和新物理效应灵敏度的关键因素。

Abstract: The forward--backward asymmetry ($A_{FB}$) in light-quark production is a sensitive probe of the electroweak sector and potential flavour-dependent BSM effects. We present a study of $e^+e^- \rightarrow s\bar{s}$ at $\sqrt{s}=250$ GeV at future linear colliders, using full ILD simulation and reconstruction tools for ILC and LCF@CERN.
  We assess the impact of particle identification on charge reconstruction and $A_{FB}$ extraction, considering software improvements using Comprehensive PID (CPID) for optimal $dE/dx$ usage, as well as hardware scenarios including cluster counting ($dN/dx$) and ideal TPC performance. Statistical precision gains are evaluated, with corrections for charge misidentification and acceptance applied.
  Results indicate that precise $A_{FB}^{s\bar{s}}$ measurements are feasible and that advanced PID is key to maximising sensitivity to electroweak and new-physics effects.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 洛伦兹不变性是粒子物理标准模型（Standard Model）和广义相对论（General Relativity）的基础对称性。检验其有效性为在普朗克尺度（Planck scale）附近寻找新物理提供了直接途径。

Method: 使用KM3NeT/ORCA探测器的部分配置（包含六个探测单元）收集的1.4年大气中微子（atmospheric neutrino）数据进行各向同性洛伦兹不变性破坏（isotropic Lorentz invariance violation）的搜索。

Result: 未发现洛伦兹不变性破坏的证据，从而对一组各向同性洛伦兹不变性破坏系数（isotropic Lorentz invariance violating coefficients）设置了竞争性的限制。

Conclusion: 获得的限制参数补充并扩展了现有的实验约束，为在普朗克尺度附近寻找新物理提供了重要数据支持。

Abstract: Lorentz invariance is a fundamental symmetry underlying both the Standard Model of particle physics and General Relativity. Testing its validity provides a direct means of searching for new physics emerging near the Planck scale. A search for isotropic Lorentz invariance violation with 1.4 years of atmospheric neutrino data collected by a partial configuration of the KM3NeT/ORCA detector comprising six detection units is presented. No evidence for such violation is found; thus, competitive limits are set on a subset of isotropic Lorentz invariance violating coefficients, which complement and extend existing experimental constraints.

# cond-mat.stat-mech [[Back]](#toc)

### [36] [Relaxation to nonequilibrium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03490)
*Christian Maes,Karel Netočný*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究描述了向稳态宏观非平衡态弛豫的演化方程结构，将其表征为Onsager-Machlup作用的非平衡非线性扩展的零成本流，建立了宏观涨落与响应之间的内在联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解向稳态宏观非平衡态弛豫的演化方程结构，建立宏观涨落与响应之间的内在联系，并推广经典的平衡态弛豫理论至非平衡条件。

Method: 该方法基于两个核心要素：局部细致平衡原理（local detailed balance）用于识别相关热力学力，以及将frenesy分解为勒让德对（Legendre pair）的规范分解。通过非平衡非线性扩展的Onsager-Machlup作用，将演化表征为零成本流。

Result: 研究揭示了拉格朗日量的时间对称分量——frenesy——在给定外力下塑造宏观演化结构的关键作用。该结果可解释为GENERIC形式主义（GENERIC formalism）向稳态非平衡条件的非平衡推广。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了向稳态非平衡条件弛豫的演化方程结构理论框架，将平衡态弛豫的耗散梯度流叠加哈密顿流的描述推广至非平衡情形，深化了对宏观非平衡动力学与涨落之间关系的理解。

Abstract: We describe the structure of evolution equations for the relaxation toward a steady macroscopic nonequilibrium state. The evolution is characterized as the zero-cost flow for a nonequilibrium and nonlinear extension of the Onsager-Machlup action governing macroscopic dynamical fluctuations, thus following the intrinsic connection between macroscopic fluctuations and response. The approach hinges on two main elements: the principle of local detailed balance, which identifies the relevant thermodynamic forces, and the canonical decomposition of the frenesy into a Legendre pair. Notably, it is the time-symmetric component of the Lagrangian, the frenesy, that shapes the structure of the macroscopic evolution for given forcing. The results can be interpreted as a nonequilibrium generalization for relaxation to steady nonequilibrium conditions of the well-established GENERIC formalism, in which relaxation to equilibrium is described by a dissipative gradient flow superimposed on a Hamiltonian flow.

</details>


### [37] [Adding noise and scaling forces to speed up the Langevin clock](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03620)
*Prithviraj Basak,Stephen Whitelam,John Bechhoefer*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 通过光学镊子捕获胶体粒子的实验，验证了通过同时缩放确定性力并添加外部噪声来提高朗之万（Langevin）动力学系统有效迁移率或时钟速率的理论方案。该方法还能使非平衡系统更接近热平衡，并提高非平衡功关系中自由能差值的计算精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在实验验证最近提出的理论方案：通过同时缩放确定性力并添加外部噪声，提高朗之万（Langevin）动力学系统的有效迁移率或时钟速率。这一方法对于新兴的热力学计算（thermodynamic computing）领域具有重要意义，该领域利用受朗之万动力学支配的随机设备进行低能耗计算。

Method: 采用光学镊子（optical tweezer）捕获胶体粒子（colloidal particle）进行实验研究。通过同时缩放确定性力（deterministic forces）并添加外部噪声（external noise）来实现朗之万时钟重缩放（Langevin clock rescaling）。

Result: 实验证实了通过同时缩放确定性力并添加外部噪声可以提高系统的有效迁移率或时钟速率。同时验证了推论：受时间相关协议驱动的非平衡系统能够更接近热平衡（thermal equilibrium）。作为应用，该方法能够更精确地从非平衡功关系（nonequilibrium work relations）中恢复自由能差值（free-energy differences）。

Conclusion: 朗之万时钟重缩放为热力学计算领域提供了一种通用的加速计算策略。该方法通过提高随机设备的时钟速率，能够更高效地进行低能耗计算，同时保持系统接近热平衡状态。

Abstract: Using experiments on a colloidal particle trapped in an optical tweezer, we confirm a recent proposal to increase the effective mobility or clock rate of systems described by Langevin dynamics, by simultaneously scaling deterministic forces and adding external noise. A corollary, which we also confirm experimentally, is that a system driven out of equilibrium by a time-dependent protocol can remain closer to thermal equilibrium. As an application, we demonstrate more precise recovery of free-energy differences from nonequilibrium work relations. Langevin clock rescaling provides a general strategy for accelerating calculations in the emerging field of thermodynamic computing, which uses stochastic devices governed by Langevin dynamics to do low-energy calculations.

</details>


### [38] [Ising Models of Cooperativity in Muscle Contraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03866)
*Elaheh Saadat,Matthieu Caruel,Stefano Gherardini,Ilaria Morotti,Matteo Marcello,Marco Caremani,Marco Linari,Ivan Latella,Stefano Ruffo*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出一维伊辛模型（one-dimensional Ising model）解释横纹肌细丝激活的协同机制，该模型仅需钙离子浓度和肌球蛋白马达作用力两个参数，成功预测实验数据并解释药物Omecamtiv Mecarbil的抗协同效应。

Motivation: 横纹肌收缩受细丝（含肌动蛋白）和粗丝（含肌球蛋白）双重机制调控。细丝激活涉及钙离子结合肌钙蛋白引发的构象变化，以及肌球蛋白马达附着后的协同激活扩散机制，需要理论模型阐明这种协同性的物理基础。

Method: 引入一维伊辛模型表征细丝激活的协同机制，模型仅使用两个参数：与钙离子浓度相关的参数，以及受温度调制的附着肌球蛋白马达作用力参数。该模型能确定肌动蛋白-肌球蛋白相互作用在调控单元（regulatory unit）七个肌动蛋白单体之外的关联长度范围。

Result: 模型预测在任意作用力下，肌动蛋白-肌球蛋白相互作用可延伸至调控单元七个肌动蛋白单体之外的2-7个单体范围。理论预测成功通过实验数据验证，并解释了特定药物Omecamtiv Mecarbil阻碍细丝激活条件下的抗协同机制（anti-cooperativity mechanism）。

Conclusion: 一维伊辛模型有效阐明了细丝激活的协同机制物理基础，仅需钙离子浓度和肌球蛋白作用力两个参数即可描述系统行为。模型不仅解释正常条件下的协同激活，还能解释药物诱导的抗协同效应，为理解肌肉收缩调控提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Regulation of contraction in striated muscle is controlled by a dual mechanism involving both thin filaments containing actin and thick filaments containing myosin. The thin filament is activated by calcium ions binding to troponin, leading to tropomyosin azimuthal displacement which allows the activation of a regulatory unit (composed of one troponin, one tropomyosin and seven actin monomers) that exposes the actin sites for interaction with the myosin motors. Motor attachment to actin contributes to spreading activation within and beyond a regulatory unit along the thin filament through a cooperative mechanism. We introduce a one-dimensional Ising model to elucidate the mechanism of cooperativity in thin filament activation in relation to the force generated by the attached myosin motor. The model characterizes thin filament activation and cooperativity using only two parameters: one related to calcium concentration and the other to the force exerted by the attached myosin motor, which is modulated by temperature. At any force, the model is able to determine the extent of actin-myosin interactions on a correlation length ranging from two to seven actin monomers in addition to the seven actin monomers of the regulatory unit. Our theoretical predictions are successfully tested on experimental data, and our tests also include the condition of hindered filament activation by the use of the specific drug Omecamtiv Mecarbil (OM). According to our model, the effect of OM results in an anti-cooperativity mechanism accounting for the experimental data.

### [39] [Pushing-Induced Arrest Across Lattices and Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04048)
*I. Shitrit,O. lauber Bonomo,S. Reuveni*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了示踪剂-介质相互作用在三维空间中超越经典模型的输运现象，特别是障碍物推动效应如何消除渗透（percolation），并提出了基于涌现捕获机制的新解释框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 示踪剂与介质间的相互作用可产生超越经典模型的输运现象，例如障碍物推动（obstacle pushing）能消除渗透现象。现有理论对此效应的解释在三维空间中失效，需要新的理论框架来理解这一现象。

Method: 研究通过分析示踪剂在介质中的动力学行为，识别出限制机制由涌现的捕获（emergent trapping）事件主导，这些事件表现为具有恒定每步概率的罕见"门关闭"（door-closing）过程，导致指数型生存概率。

Result: 研究发现捕获机制产生指数型生存概率，从而能够从扩散常数和捕获概率的短时估计预测时间依赖的均方位移（mean-squared displacement）。这为跨晶格和维度的推动诱导停滞（pushing-induced arrest）提供了最小描述框架。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了基于涌现捕获事件的理论框架，成功解释了三维空间中推动诱导停滞现象，提供了从短时动力学参数预测长期输运行为的有效方法，统一了不同维度和晶格结构下的描述。

Abstract: Tracer-media interactions can give rise to transport phenomena beyond classical models; e.g., obstacle pushing can eliminate percolation. We demonstrate that the existing explanation of this effect fails in 3D. We show that confinement is governed by emergent trapping-rare door-closing events with constant probability per step-yielding exponential survival. This allows prediction of the time-dependent mean-squared displacement from short-time estimates of the diffusion constant and trapping probability, providing a minimal description of pushing-induced arrest across lattices and dimensions.

### [40] [Mermin's dielectric function and the f-sum rule](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04054)
*Thomas Chuna,Jan Vorberger,Thomas Gawne,Tobias Dornheim,Michael S. Murillo*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文揭示了Mermin介电函数模型中的矩闭合问题，指出其f求和规则（f-sum rule）的满足性取决于碰撞频率的具体形式，并分析了原始模型与修正模型在该规则上的表现差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Mermin介电函数模型因采用连续性方程约束而被广泛认为满足f求和规则，但本文识别出该模型在连续性方程使用中存在矩闭合问题，需要重新审视其理论基础的完整性。

Method: 通过分析Mermin模型推导过程中的矩闭合问题，对比原始模型与Chuna和Murillo提出的"completed Mermin"修正模型，并系统检验不同碰撞频率形式下f求和规则的满足情况。

Result: 研究发现：Mermin模型中的碰撞频率若按ω比例缩放则违反f求和规则，而恒定实正碰撞频率理论上满足该规则，但数值计算中因积分上限收敛缓慢而表现出明显违反；含恒定虚部的碰撞频率同样导致规则违反。

Conclusion: Mermin模型通过优化碰撞频率拟合数据时，f求和规则并非固有满足，需要施加约束条件；即使理论上满足该规则，数值计算中的偏差也应纳入误差估计，以确保模型预测的可靠性。

Abstract: Mermin's dielectric function [N.D. Mermin, Phys. Rev. B 1, 2362 (1970)] is widely assumed to satisfy the f-sum rule because he constrains his ansatz with the continuity equation. However, we identify a moment-closure problem in Mermin's use of the continuity equation. Further, we show that the Mermin's model can be derived without invoking continuity. We describe how other approaches such as the ``completed Mermin'' model of Chuna and Murillo [Phys. Rev. E 111, 035206 (2025)] remedy this closure issue. We then inspect the f-sum rule for both the original and completed Mermin models and find for the Mermin ansatz that collision frequencies scaling as $ω$ must violate the f-sum rule, whereas constant, real, positive collision frequencies will satisfy it, with the caveat that, in practice, convergence with respect to the upper integration limit $ω_{\max}$ is sufficiently slow that finite-domain numerical evaluations exhibit apparent violations, regardless of wavenumber $q$. We also find that collision frequencies with constant imaginary components cause f-sum rule violations. We conclude that if Mermin's model is fit to data via optimizing its collision frequency, then the f-sum rule is not inherently satisfied; constraints, though broad, are needed in order to assume the f-sum rule is satisfied. Further, if the f-sum rule is theoretically satisfied, but violations still appear, then these deviations ought to be included in the error estimates.

</details>


### [41] [Kinetic Theory of Chiral Active Disks: Odd Transport and Torque Density](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04273)
*Raphael Maire,Alessandro Petrini,Umberto Marini Bettolo Marconi,Lorenzo Caprini*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个最小化的二维硬盘气体模型，其中手性仅来源于碰撞诱导的横向冲量，通过玻尔兹曼-恩斯科格描述推导了非线性流体动力学方程，并在稀薄极限下获得了奇粘度、奇热导率和奇自扩散系数等输运系数的解析预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性流体（chiral fluids）的宇称奇输运（parity-odd transport）是其核心特征，但相关解析预测较为缺乏。该研究旨在建立一个最小化的动力学模型，为手性流体的系统粗粒化提供基础，并为更广泛手性系统中的奇输运现象提供可处理的基准。

Method: 引入一个二维硬盘气体（hard-disk gas）模型，其中手性源于碰撞诱导的横向冲量（collision-induced transverse impulse）。基于颗粒自旋体（granular spinners）的启发，碰撞是耗散的，并通过接触点的固定切向"踢力"（tangential kick）注入轨道角动量。从玻尔兹曼-恩斯科格（Boltzmann-Enskog）描述出发，推导了密度、动量和温度的非线性流体动力学方程。

Result: 研究表明手性产生了一个对应于非零扭矩密度（torque density）的反称均匀应力（antisymmetric homogeneous stress）。在稀薄极限下，通过查普曼-恩斯科格展开（Chapman-Enskog expansion）获得了输运系数的解析预测，包括奇粘度（odd viscosity）、奇热导率（odd thermal conductivity）和奇自扩散系数（odd self-diffusivity），这些预测与数值模拟结果吻合良好。

Conclusion: 这个最小化的动力学模型可以作为手性流体系统粗粒化的基础，并为理解更广泛手性系统中的奇输运现象提供了一个可处理的基准模型，有助于深入探究宇称奇输运的物理机制。

Abstract: Parity-odd transport is a central signature of chiral fluids, yet analytical predictions are sparse. Here, we introduce a minimal two-dimensional hard-disk gas in which chirality arises solely from a collision-induced transverse impulse. Motivated by granular spinners, collisions are dissipative and inject orbital angular momentum through a fixed tangential ``kick'' at contact. Starting from a Boltzmann-Enskog description, we derive nonlinear hydrodynamic equations for density, momentum, and temperature, and show that chirality generates an antisymmetric homogeneous stress corresponding to a nonzero torque density. In the dilute limit, a Chapman-Enskog expansion yields analytical predictions for transport coefficients, including odd viscosity, odd thermal conductivity, and odd self-diffusivity, in good agreement with numerical simulations. This minimal kinetic model can serve as a foundation for systematic coarse-graining of chiral fluids and as a tractable benchmark for gaining insight into odd transport across a broader class of chiral systems.

</details>

### [42] [Cohomological Hall algebras of one-dimensional sheaves on surfaces and Yangians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03386)
*Duiliu-Emanuel Diaconescu,Mauro Porta,Francesco Sala,Olivier Schiffmann,Eric Vasserot*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 该论文首次代数刻画了与光滑曲面X上沿固定曲线Z的凝聚层修正相关的上同调Hecke算子代数，建立了与Yangian的直接联系。主要结果展示了当X为Kleinian奇点解消时，等变幂零上同调Hall代数与相应仿射ADE李代数Yangian的完备正半部分之间的显式同构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立代数几何中上同调Hall代数与量子群理论中Yangian之间的深刻联系。具体而言，旨在刻画光滑曲面X上沿固定曲线Z的凝聚层修正相关的上同调Hecke算子代数结构，并揭示其与Yangian的对应关系。

Method: 方法基于作者先前发展的等变幂零上同调Hall代数理论。主要工具包括：(i) 描述t-结构序列收敛时上同调Hall代数行为的"连续性"定理；(ii) 任意箭图Q的多参数Yangian定义；(iii) 辫子群在Yangian上的代数作用与在等变二维上同调Hall代数上作用的关联定理。

Result: 主要结果证明：当X为Kleinian奇点解消（如X = T*P^1）且Z为例外除子时，存在显式同构𝐇𝐀^T_X,Z ≃ 𝕐^+_∞，其中𝕐^+_∞是对应仿射ADE李代数𝔤的仿射Yangian的完备非标准正半部分。同时，𝐇𝐀^T_X,Z的生成元（由零维层子叠的基本类和Z上线丛推前的基本类给出）被显式表达为Yangian生成元。

Conclusion: 该研究首次实现了与曲面曲线对(X,Z)相关的上同调Hecke算子代数的代数刻画，并建立了其与Yangian的显式对应。这一结果为理解几何对象与量子代数结构之间的深层联系提供了新的视角，所发展的工具方法在相关领域具有独立价值。

Abstract: This paper provides the first algebraic characterization of an algebra of cohomological Hecke operators associated with modifications of coherent sheaves on a smooth surface $X$ along a fixed proper curve $Z \subset X$ (possibly singular and reducible), establishing a direct connection with Yangians. It is based on the theory of equivariant nilpotent cohomological Hall algebras $\mathbf{HA}^T_{X,Z}$, developed by the same authors.
  More precisely, let $X$ be a resolution of a Kleinian singularity (for example, $X = T^\ast\mathbb{P}^1$) and let $Z$ be the exceptional divisor. One of the main results of this paper is an explicit isomorphism $\mathbf{HA}^T_{X,Z} \simeq \mathbb{Y}^+_\infty$, where $\mathbb{Y}^+_\infty$ is a completed, nonstandard, positive half of the affine Yangian $\mathbb{Y}(\mathfrak{g})$ of the corresponding affine ADE Lie algebra $\mathfrak{g}$. Furthermore, the generators of $\mathbf{HA}^T_{X,Z}$--given by fundamental classes of substacks of zero-dimensional sheaves and of pushforwards of line bundles on $Z$--are expressed explicitly in terms of Yangian generators.
  Our main tools, which may be of independent interest, are: (i) a `continuity' theorem describing the behavior of cohomological Hall algebras of objects in the heart of $t$-structures $τ_n$ when the sequence $(τ_n)_n$ converges, in an appropriate sense, to a fixed $t$-structure $τ_\infty$; (ii) the definition of a multi-parameter Yangian $\mathbb{Y}_Q$ for an arbitrary quiver $Q$, given by generators and relations; (iii) a theorem relating the algebraic action of the braid group $B_Q$ on the Yangian $\mathbb{Y}_Q$ to the action of $B_Q$ on the equivariant 2-dimensional cohomological Hall algebra $\mathbf{HA}^T_Q$ of $Q$, where the latter can be described in terms of derived reflection functors of the bounded derived category of modules over the preprojective algebra of $Q$.

*Wadim Gerner,Anouk Nicolopoulos-Salle,Diego Pereira Botelho*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在仿星器（stellarator）设计中，线圈绕组表面（coil winding surfaces）上的电流分布（current distributions）塑造磁场。本研究旨在解释线圈优化中关键特征——中心和鞍点区域（centre and saddle point regions）的出现机制。

Method: 针对不同几何形状的线圈绕组表面建立理论框架：对于环形（toroidal）表面，证明二分原理（dichotomy principle）；对于分段圆柱（piecewise cylinders）表面，分析边界条件对电流分布的影响。

Result: 对于环形表面，电流分布要么同时包含中心和鞍点区域，要么处处非零。对于分段圆柱表面，当两个边界圆上的电流方向相反时，中心和鞍点出现，且除有限多条外，所有场线（field lines）都是周期性的。当电流分布存在调和势（harmonic potential）时，所有场线都是闭合极向轨道（closed poloidal orbits）。

Conclusion: 这些结果为绕组表面上的电流模式提供了理论见解，对线圈设计策略及其简化具有重要启示，为仿星器优化提供了理论基础。

Abstract: In stellarator design, the coil winding surfaces $Σ\subset\mathbb R^3$ support current distributions $j$ that shape the magnetic field. This work provides a theoretical framework explaining the emergence of centre and saddle point regions, a key feature in coil optimisation. For coil winding surfaces with a toroidal shape, we prove a dichotomy principle: the current distribution has both centre and saddle point regions or is no-where vanishing. For coil winding surfaces that consist of piecewise cylinders, we show that if $j$ is oppositely oriented on the two boundary circles, centre and saddle points appear, and all but finitely many field lines of $j$ are periodic. When $j$ admits a harmonic potential, all field lines are closed poloidal orbits. These results offer insights into current patterns on winding surfaces, with implications for coil design strategies and their simplification.

### [44] [Effect of magnetic drift on the stability structure of the ambipolar condition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03656)
*Keiji Fujita,Shinsuke Satake*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 在非轴对称等离子体中，双极条件（ambipolar condition）可能存在多个解（multiple roots）。研究显示，轨道模型中包含磁漂移（magnetic drift）会显著改变势能景观（potential landscape），影响解的选择，并可能解释不同模拟结果之间的差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在解释非轴对称等离子体中双极径向电场（ambipolar radial electric field）模拟结果与实验观测之间的差异。特别是，不同轨道模型（orbit models）的模拟结果存在不一致，需要探究其物理机制。

Method: 通过将双极电场的演化描述为双稳态势（bistable potential）中的动力学过程，分析磁漂移（magnetic drift）对势能景观（potential landscape）的影响。研究考察了势阱（potential wells）相对深度对实现解（realized root）的决定作用。

Result: 包含磁漂移的轨道模型会显著改变势能景观，从而影响双极条件解的选择。这一效应为不同轨道模型模拟结果之间的差异，以及模拟与实验观测之间的不一致提供了可能的解释。

Conclusion: 双极电场可能比先前预期更容易受到涨落（fluctuations）的影响，表明噪声诱导状态转变（noise-induced state transitions）具有潜在相关性。磁漂移在决定非轴对称等离子体中双极电场剖面方面起着关键作用。

Abstract: In non-axisymmetric plasmas, the ambipolar condition may have multiple roots.
  In such cases, the evolution of the ambipolar electric field can be described by the dynamics in a bistable potential, where the relative depth of the potential wells primarily determines the realized root.
  In this study, we show that the inclusion of the magnetic drift in the orbit model can significantly modify the potential landscape and affect root selection.
  This effect provides a possible explanation for discrepancies between simulation results obtained using different orbit models, as well as between simulations and experimental observations of ambipolar radial electric field profiles.
  Further, the analysis suggests that the ambipolar electric field may be more susceptible to fluctuations than previously expected, indicating the potential relevance of noise-induced state transitions.

</details>

### [45] [TritonDFT: Automating DFT with a Multi-Agent Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03372)
*Zhengding Hu,Kuntal Talit,Zhen Wang,Haseeb Ahmad,Yichen Lin,Prabhleen Kaur,Christopher Lane,Elizabeth A. Peterson,Zhiting Hu,Elizabeth A. Nowadnick,Yufei Ding*

TL;DR: TritonDFT是一个多智能体框架，通过专家策划的可扩展工作流设计、帕累托感知参数推断和多源知识增强，实现高效准确的密度泛函理论（DFT）计算执行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 密度泛函理论（Density Functional Theory, DFT）是材料科学的基石，但在实践中执行DFT需要协调复杂、多步骤的工作流。现有工具和基于大语言模型（LLM-based）的解决方案仅能自动化部分步骤，缺乏对完整工作流自动化、多样化任务适应以及DFT配置中精度-成本权衡优化的支持。

Method: 提出了TritonDFT多智能体框架，采用专家策划的可扩展工作流设计、帕累托感知参数推断（Pareto-aware parameter inference）和多源知识增强（multi-source knowledge augmentation）。同时引入了DFTBench基准测试，用于评估智能体在科学专业知识、权衡优化、高性能计算（HPC）知识和成本效率等多维度的能力。

Result: TritonDFT提供了用于实际应用的开源用户界面，相关网站和源代码及基准测试套件均已公开可用。

Conclusion: 该研究通过TritonDFT框架解决了DFT工作流自动化的关键挑战，实现了高效准确的DFT执行，并通过DFTBench基准测试为相关智能体系统提供了多维度的评估标准。

Abstract: Density Functional Theory (DFT) is a cornerstone of materials science, yet executing DFT in practice requires coordinating a complex, multi-step workflow. Existing tools and LLM-based solutions automate parts of the steps, but lack support for full workflow automation, diverse task adaptation, and accuracy-cost trade-off optimization in DFT configuration. To this end, we present TritonDFT, a multi-agent framework that enables efficient and accurate DFT execution through an expert-curated, extensible workflow design, Pareto-aware parameter inference, and multi-source knowledge augmentation. We further introduce DFTBench, a benchmark for evaluating the agent's multi-dimensional capabilities, spanning science expertise, trade0off optimization, HPC knowledge, and cost efficiency. TritonDFT provides an open user interface for real-world usage. Our website is at https://www.tritondft.com. Method: 采用非相互作用电子模型，建立了调制布洛赫态（modulated Bloch states）理论，推导了有效场方程，并通过提出广义WKB方法（GWKB）、有效质量近似（effective mass approximation）、玻尔兹曼方程（Boltzmann equation）和数值方法进行求解。

Result: 广义WKB解并非半经典方法，在完全量子体系中仍然有效；研究表明电导率、磁导率和介电常数等有效观测量在梯度介质中通常无法用张量描述；工程化的取向梯度能够精确控制朗道量子化（Landau quantization）。

Abstract: Functionally graded materials (FGMs) are composites whose composition or microstructure varies continuously in space, producing position-dependent mechanical and functional properties. In recent years, FGMs have gained significant attention due to advances in additive manufacturing, which enable precise spatial control of composition and orientation. However, their graded, aperiodic structure breaks the assumptions of Bloch's theorem, making first-principles electronic and electromagnetic calculations challenging. Here we develop an ab initio quantum theoretical framework for the electromagnetic properties of FGMs. Using a non-interacting electron model, we formulate a theory of modulated Bloch states, derive effective field equations, and solve them by proposing a generalized WKB (GWKB) method, an effective mass approximation, the Boltzmann equation, and numerical approaches. Our GWKB solution is not semiclassical but remains valid in the fully quantum regime. We show that effective observables such as conductivity, magnetic permeability, and electric permittivity generally do not admit a tensorial description in graded media, and that engineered orientational gradients enable precise control of Landau quantization. As a device example, we further develop a theory of graded p-n junctions with enhanced electronic tunability. This framework lays the quantum foundation for predictive design of graded composite materials, enabling AI-accelerated discovery of next-generation functional architectures.

Abstract: Controllable doping in AlN and its alloys is essential for deep-ultraviolet light sources. We report first-principles calculations demonstrating that strain engineering can result in a reduction in ionization energies. The donor levels for $\mathrm{S_N}$ and $\mathrm{Se_N}$ shift closer to the conduction-band minimum (CBM) under in-plane tensile strains, driven by a downward shift of the CBM. The most widely used donor, $\mathrm{Si_{Al}}$, forms a $DX$ center in AlN. We find that a 2.5% in-plane tensile strain (which would be induced by pseudomorphic growth on GaN in experiment) shifts the ($+/-$) transition level from 271 meV to 98 meV below the CBM, which would enhance the electron concentration by three orders of magnitude. These results demonstrate that strain engineering offers an effective route to enhance doping levels in AlN.
