### [146] [Observational constraints on Luciano-Saridakis entropic cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03568)
*Matías Leizerovich,Susana J. Landau,Giuseppe Gaetano Luciano,Andreas Papatriantafyllou,Emmanuel N. Saridakis*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文首次对Luciano-Saridakis广义熵（generalized entropy）宇宙学模型进行观测约束，发现该模型能同时满足Pantheon$^+$、SH0ES和CMB数据约束，在背景层面具有缓解哈勃张力（Hubble tension）的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Luciano-Saridakis提出的广义熵通过两个独立的熵指数扩展了标准Boltzmann-Gibbs和Bekenstein-Hawking框架，在引力-热力学对应关系中产生修正的宇宙学动力学。该模型需要首次观测验证以评估其作为有效暗能量（dark energy）模型的可行性。

Method: 研究聚焦于α_δ=0情况，在背景层面使用多种观测数据约束模型：宇宙计时器（Cosmic Chronometers）、经SH0ES校准的Pantheon$^+$ Ia型超新星、DESI DR2的BAO测量以及压缩的Planck 2018 CMB信息。

Result: 模型对组合数据集提供了统计上稳健的拟合，能同时满足Pantheon$^+$、SH0ES和CMB偏移参数约束，而ΛCDM模型无法做到这一点。虽然熵参数接近标准值，但在所考虑的受限参数空间中，ΛCDM极限在2σ水平被排除。

Conclusion: Luciano-Saridakis熵宇宙学模型是标准模型的一个可行扩展，在背景层面具有缓解哈勃张力的潜力，为基于热力学原理的暗能量模型提供了观测支持。

Abstract: A recently proposed generalized entropy by Luciano and Saridakis extends the standard Boltzmann-Gibbs and Bekenstein-Hawking framework through a microscopically motivated construction involving two independent entropic exponents. When applied within the gravity-thermodynamics correspondence, this entropy leads to a modified cosmological dynamics that can be interpreted as an effective dark energy sector of entropic origin, while recovering $Λ$CDM in appropriate limits. In this work, we perform the first observational confrontation of the resulting entropic cosmology at the background level. Focusing on the case $α_δ=0$, we constrain the model using Cosmic Chronometers, Pantheon$^+$ Type Ia supernovae calibrated with SH0ES, BAO measurements from DESI DR2 and compressed Planck 2018 CMB information. We find that the model yields a statistically robust fit to the combined data sets and can simultaneously satisfy Pantheon$^+$, SH0ES and CMB shift-parameter constraints, unlike $Λ$CDM. Although the entropic parameters remain close to their standard values, the $Λ$CDM limit is excluded at the $2σ$ level within the restricted parameter space considered. These results indicate that the Luciano-Saridakis entropic cosmology offers a viable extension of the standard model with the potential to alleviate the Hubble tension at the background level.

</details>


### [147] [Cosmology with the line-of-sight shear of strong gravitational lenses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03441)
*Pierre Fleury,Daniel Johnson,Théo Duboscq,Natalie B. Hogg,Julien Larena*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文提出利用强引力透镜的视线剪切（line-of-sight shear）作为新的宇宙学探针，将标准3×2点相关函数方法扩展为6×2点方案，并证明在第四阶段巡天中该信号能以高信噪比被探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 第四阶段（stage-IV）光度巡天预计将探测到超过十万个强引力透镜（strong gravitational lenses）。本文旨在利用强透镜的弱透镜扰动，特别是视线剪切（line-of-sight shear），作为一种新的宇宙学探针。

Method: 提出利用强透镜的视线剪切定义三个新的相关函数：视线剪切自相关、视线剪切与星系位置相关、视线剪切与星系形状相关，从而将标准3×2点相关方法推广到6×2点方案。设计了这些新相关函数的估计器，并推导了其期望值与物质功率谱（matter power spectrum）的函数关系。

Result: 推导了6×2点相关方案的完整协方差矩阵（covariance matrix）的解析表达式。考虑第四阶段强透镜样本的各种情景，证明即使在最悲观情况下，强透镜视线剪切携带的宇宙学信息也能以非常高的信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio）被探测到。

Conclusion: 强引力透镜是极具前景的宇宙学探针，其与星系位置和形状的协同作用也有助于减轻第四阶段巡天中的系统误差（systematics）。

Abstract: Stage-IV photometric galaxy surveys are designed to measure the position and shapes of billions of galaxies. Their aim is to characterise the large-scale distribution of matter in the Universe using galaxy clustering and weak gravitational lensing. As a byproduct, stage-IV surveys are expected to detect more than a hundred thousand strong gravitational lenses. In this article, we propose the use of weak-lensing perturbations to strong lenses, specifically their line-of-sight (LOS) shear, as a cosmological probe. This new observable allows us to define three new correlation functions: the LOS shear with itself, with galaxy positions, and with galaxy shapes, thereby promoting the standard $3\times 2$pt correlation method to a $6\times 2$pt scheme. We design estimators for these new correlation functions and determine their expectation values as a function of the matter power spectrum. We then derive the analytical expression for the full covariance matrix of the $6\times 2$pt correlation scheme. Considering various scenarios for the stage-IV strong-lensing samples, we demonstrate that the cosmological information carried by the LOS shear of strong lenses will be detectable with a very high signal-to-noise ratio, even in the most pessimistic of cases. Strong lenses are thus extremely promising cosmological probes, whose synergy with galaxy positions and shapes should also contribute to mitigating systematics in stage-IV surveys.

</details>


### [148] [Illuminating the dark universe in the multi-messenger era](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03446)
*Philippe Brax,Anne-Christine Davis,Md Riajul Haque,Cédric Jockel,Gaetano Lambiase,Michiru Uwabo-Niibo,Mohsen Khodadi,Tanmay Kumar Poddar,Laura Sagunski,Luca Visinelli,Jun Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该综述探讨了如何利用多信使天文学（multi-messenger astronomy）和现代天体物理观测来探测暗物质（dark matter）候选者和修改引力理论（modified gravity），涵盖从太阳系到宇宙学尺度的约束条件，并展望了未来实验的探测前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多信使天文学进入精确时代，结合现代天体物理、宇宙学和引力波观测，日益指向存在无法用粒子物理标准模型（Standard Model）和广义相对论（General Relativity）解释的"暗"（dark）成分。需要探索标准物理的扩展，并研究如何利用观测数据探测新粒子和相互作用。

Method: 综述方法包括：考虑从太阳系测试到星系和宇宙学观测的广泛尺度；研究传统暗物质候选者如弱相互作用大质量粒子（weakly interacting massive particles）和替代方案如超轻场（ultralight fields）和原初黑洞（primordial black holes）；分析来自致密天体（compact objects）如中子星、黑洞、脉冲星和磁星的观测约束；研究涉及额外标量场（scalar fields）的广义相对论扩展及其对引力波信号和原初黑洞随机背景的影响。

Result: 当前观测已对暗物质和修改引力模型（modified-gravity models）施加了显著限制。通过分析暗物质在致密天体中的捕获和积累（可改变质量、半径和潮汐形变能力等性质），以及暗物质衰变为标准模型粒子的情景，获得了重要的约束条件。

Conclusion: 即将进行的实验和天文台预计将通过改进对粒子质量和相互作用强度的约束，进一步探测或发现此类新物理。多信使天文学和现代观测技术为探索暗物质和修改引力理论提供了强大的工具。

Abstract: The precision era of multi-messenger astronomy, together with modern astrophysical, cosmological, and gravitational wave observations, increasingly points toward the existence of a ``dark" sector that cannot be explained within the framework of the Standard Model of particle physics and General Relativity. In this review, we explore extensions of standard physics and examine how observational data can be used to probe new particles and interactions. We consider a wide range of scales, from Solar System tests to galactic and cosmological observations, and investigate both conventional dark matter candidates, such as weakly interacting massive particles, and alternative scenarios including ultralight fields and primordial black holes. We discuss constraints derived from compact objects such as neutron stars, black holes, pulsars, and magnetars observations as well as from high-energy astrophysical phenomena. In addition, we analyze extensions of General Relativity involving additional scalar fields and their impact on gravitational wave signals and stochastic backgrounds from primordial black holes. We also study the capture and accumulation of dark matter in compact objects, which can alter properties such as mass, radius, and tidal deformability, and consider scenarios in which dark matter decays into Standard Model particles. While current observations already place significant limits on dark matter and modified-gravity models, upcoming experiments and observatories are expected to further probe or discover such new physics by improving constraints on particle masses and interaction strengths.

</details>


### [149] [Excursion-set for Primordial Black Holes I: white noise and moving barrier](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04185)
*Pierre Auclair,Baptiste Blachier,Vincent Vennin*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究为远足集形式主义（excursion-set formalism）在原始黑洞质量分布计算中的有效性进行辩护，回应了关于噪声相关性和云中云（cloud-in-cloud）效应相关性的两项批评，并建立了同步表面采样和移动边界问题的数值框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对远足集形式主义在计算原始黑洞（primordial black holes, PBHs）质量分布时面临的两项批评：一是随机游走中的噪声被误认为有色噪声（colored noise），二是云中云效应被认为不相关。本研究旨在澄清这些误解并证明该方法的必要性。

Method: 通过分析哈勃交叉表面（Hubble-crossing surface）采样与同步表面（synchronous surface）采样的差异，证明前者导致伪相关问题。采用同步表面采样解决了噪声相关问题，并建立了处理移动边界（moving barrier）首次通过时间（first-passage-time）问题的高效数值框架。

Result: 研究表明：1) 若傅里叶模式不相关，噪声严格为白噪声；2) 哈勃交叉表面采样无法使用密度离散度作为时间变量；3) 同步表面采样同时解决了这两个问题；4) 对于具有增强连续模式的宽功率谱，云中云效应不可忽略；5) 忽略边界演化的Press-Schechter估计即使在无云中云效应时也会失效。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了远足集形式主义在现实原始黑洞形成场景中的稳健性和必要性，澄清了相关批评的误解，并为处理移动边界问题提供了有效的数值解决方案。

Abstract: In the excursion-set formalism, the mass distribution of primordial black holes (PBHs) is derived from the first-passage time of a random walk describing the density contrast as the coarse-graining scale varies. We address two recent criticisms that have been raised about this approach. First, it was argued that the random walks are subject to colored (i.e. correlated over time) noise, making the first-passage-time problem cumbersome. We show that this arises from an incorrect separation of drift and noise when sampling on the Hubble-crossing surface: if Fourier modes are uncorrelated, the noise is strictly white. Moreover, sampling along the Hubble-crossing surface precludes using the density dispersion as a time variable, explaining the reported pathologies. Sampling instead on a synchronous surface removes both issues. This requires solving a first-passage-time problem with a moving barrier, for which we provide an efficient numerical framework. Second, it was suggested that cloud-in-cloud (i.e. that large black holes may engulf smaller ones) is irrelevant for PBHs and that the excursion set is therefore not needed. While valid for widely separated scales, this statement fails for broad power spectra with enhanced continua of modes. We further show that Press-Schechter estimates neglecting boundary evolution can break down even without cloud-in-cloud effects. Our results establish the robustness and necessity of the excursion-set formalism in realistic PBH formation scenarios.

</details>


### [150] [Wave-Optics Imprints of Dark Matter Subhalos on Strongly Lensed Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04267)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在利用强引力透镜化引力波中的波动光学效应（wave-optics effects），作为探测暗物质子结构（dark matter substructure）的新型干涉测量工具。该方法可提供电磁测量无法触及的亚星系质量尺度暗物质结构的直接观测窗口。

Method: 通过计算引力波在统计生成的冷暗物质子晕群体中传播的完整衍射积分（diffraction integral），量化了在激光干涉空间天线（Laser Interferometer Space Antenna, LISA）频段产生的频率依赖性放大效应。

Result: 研究发现，现实星系尺度透镜（galaxy-scale lenses）通常会在强放大图像中产生百分比级别的振幅和相位畸变，主要由质量范围在$10^4$-$10^7\,M_{\odot}$的子晕引起。这些特征在标准冷暗物质范式（standard cold dark matter paradigm）中自然出现，可在高信噪比LISA事件中被探测到。

Conclusion: 强引力透镜化引力波为探测亚星系质量尺度的暗物质结构提供了直接且互补的观测窗口，这一尺度是电磁测量无法触及的，从而开辟了暗物质子结构研究的新途径。

Abstract: Wave-optics effects in strongly lensed gravitational waves (GWs) provide a new interferometric probe of dark matter substructure. We compute the full diffraction integral for GWs propagating through statistically generated cold dark matter subhalo populations and quantify the resulting frequency-dependent amplification in the Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA) band. We show that realistic galaxy-scale lenses generically produce percent-level amplitude and phase distortions in strongly magnified images, primarily induced by subhalos in the mass range $10^4$-$10^7\,M_{\odot}$. These signatures arise naturally within the standard cold dark matter paradigm and should be detectable in high signal-to-noise LISA events. Strongly lensed GWs thus offer a direct and complementary window on dark matter structure at subgalactic mass scales inaccessible to electromagnetic measurements.

### [151] [Post-inflationary axion constraints from the Lyman-$α$ forest](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04401)
*Olga Garcia-Gallego,Vid Iršič,Matteo Viel,Martin G. Haehnelt,James S. Bolton*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究利用莱曼α森林（Lyman-α forest）通量功率谱数据，对暴胀后产生的类轴子粒子（ALPs）诱导的等曲率扰动（isocurvature perturbations）贡献进行了约束，发现了等曲率分数（f_iso）的非零贡献迹象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轴子（axion）作为最有前景的冷暗物质候选者之一，其性质需要通过天体物理研究加以约束。研究旨在利用莱曼α森林数据更新等曲率分数（isocurvature fraction）的界限，该参数量化了暴胀后产生的类轴子粒子诱导的等曲率扰动对普通功率谱的贡献。

Method: 基于Sherwood-Relics套件的新模拟，拟合高分辨率莱曼α森林通量功率谱（Lyman-α forest flux power spectrum）数据。研究考虑了星系际介质（IGM）热演化的简并效应，并采用了两种不同的噪声模型进行分析。

Result: 使用已发布的噪声模型时，发现等曲率分数的初步检测结果为f_iso = 0.0064^{+0.0012}_{-0.0014}（68%置信水平）。采用更保守的残余噪声建模时，上限放宽至f_iso < 0.0084（95%置信水平），对应类轴子温度无关质量m_a > 1.73 × 10^{-18}eV。

Conclusion: 该约束强于从高红移和低红移大尺度结构（large-scale structure）探针推导的界限，并与紫外光度函数（UV luminosity function）数据推导的约束具有竞争力。值得注意的是，当前最佳莱曼α森林数据倾向于等曲率模式（isocurvature modes）的非零贡献。

Abstract: Among the most compelling cold dark matter candidates, the axion has recently been subject to a wide range of astrophysical studies aiming to constraints its properties. We present updated bounds on the isocurvature fraction, $f_{\rm{iso}}$, which parameterizes the contribution of isocurvature perturbations induced by post-inflationary produced axion-like particles (ALPs) to the ordinary power spectrum. We use new simulations based on the Sherwood-Relics suite to fit high-resolution Lyman-$α$ forest flux power spectrum data. With the published noise model of the Lyman-$α$ forest data, we find a tentative detection of $f_{\rm{iso}}$ = ${0.0064^{+0.0012}_{-0.0014}}$ (68% C.L), after accounting for the degenerate effect of IGM thermal evolution. With a more conservative modelling of the residual noise in the data, the upper bound is weakened to $f_{\rm{iso}}< 0.0084$ (95% C.L), which translates into an ALP temperature-independent mass $m_a > 1.73 \times 10^{-18}$eV. Our constraints are stronger than bounds derived from large-scale structure probes at higher and lower redshifts and are competitive with those derived from UV luminosity function data. Interestingly, the best current Lyman-$α$ forest data prefers a non-zero contribution from isocurvature modes.

### [152] [Observational Indistinguishability and the Beginning of the Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04159)
*Daniel Linford*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 该论文对宇宙是否具有开端（cosmic beginning）持怀疑态度，通过分析确认理论错误、提出必要条件、扩展Malament-Manchak定理，并反驳归纳法反驳，论证观测数据不足以确定宇宙是否具有开端。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在探讨能否推断物理实在（physical reality）是否具有开端，针对支持宇宙开端的常见论证策略提出质疑，特别是基于个别无开端宇宙模型（beginningless cosmological models）不可信性的论证方法。

Method: 首先指出支持宇宙开端论证中的确认理论（confirmation theory）基本错误；其次提出宇宙开端的两个必要（但非充分）条件；第三，对Malament-Manchak定理进行三个扩展；最后反驳通过归纳法（induction）克服怀疑论后果的异议。

Result: 三个扩展表明，在几乎所有经典时空（classical spacetimes）中，观测者无法收集足够数据来确定经典奇点定理（singularity theorems）的应用条件是否满足，或时空是否满足宇宙开端的两个必要条件。所有过去的奇异尘埃FLRW时空（singular dust FLRW spacetimes）都有观测上无法区分的对应物，这些对应物要么在每点过去方向不包含奇点，要么不具有直观上宇宙开端所需的时间排序。

Conclusion: 论文得出否定性结论，认为无法推断物理实在是否具有开端。通过理论分析和定理扩展，论证了观测数据的局限性，支持对宇宙开端问题的怀疑立场。

Abstract: Can we infer whether all of physical reality began to exist? Several novel results are offered suggesting a negative verdict. First, a common strategy for defending a cosmic beginning involves showing that individual beginningless cosmological models are implausible. This strategy is shown to make an elementary error in confirmation theory. Second, two necessary (but not necessarily sufficient) conditions are offered for a cosmic beginning. Third, three extensions are offered to the Malament-Manchak theorems. The three extensions show that in almost all classical spacetimes, observers cannot collect sufficient data to determine whether the application conditions for the classic singularity theorems are satisfied or whether their spacetime satisfies the two necessary conditions for a cosmic beginning. Lastly, a reply is offered to the objection that the skeptical consequences of the three extensions can be overcome with induction. Importantly, all past singular dust FLRW spacetimes have observationally indistinguishable counterparts which, while sharing a number of important local properties, either do not include a singularity to the past of every point or else do not have the sort of time ordering intuitively required for a cosmic beginning.

</details>

### [153] [q-Gaussian Crossover in Overlap Spectra towards 3D Edwards-Anderson Criticality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03513)
*Yaprak Onder,Abbas Ali Saberi,Roderich Moessner*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种表征三维Edwards-Anderson自旋玻璃的光谱方法，通过分析二维截面重叠矩阵的本征值统计，发现从高温下的Wigner半圆律向临界点附近的高斯分布转变，该分布可用Tsallis统计描述，其熵指数q从-1演化到1。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在开发一种计算高效的谱统计方法来表征三维Edwards-Anderson自旋玻璃，作为多副本关联子方法（multi-replica correlator methods）的补充，为无序系统中的合作和临界现象提供新视角。

Method: 采用光谱方法（spectral approach），通过分析从二维截面构建的重叠矩阵（overlap matrices）的本征值统计，研究其谱密度分布随温度的变化，并利用Tsallis统计描述谱密度。

Result: 研究发现谱密度从高温下的Wigner半圆律（Wigner semicircle law）向自旋玻璃临界点附近的高斯分布转变，该转变在不同随机耦合分布下均可见；谱密度可用Tsallis统计描述，熵指数q从q=-1（半圆律，T=∞）演化到q=1（高斯分布，T=T_c）。

Conclusion: 高斯分布可作为自旋玻璃临界性的稳健谱指标（robust spectral indicator），谱统计方法为无序系统中的合作和临界现象提供了计算高效的新视角，而局部能级统计仍与GOE统计一致，反映标准能级排斥。

Abstract: We introduce a spectral approach to characterizing the three-dimensional Edwards-Anderson spin glass. By analyzing the eigenvalue statistics of overlap matrices constructed from two-dimensional cross-sections, we identify a crossover from the Wigner semicircle law at high temperatures towards a Gaussian distribution, which is consistently attained near the spin-glass critical point. Visible for different distributions of the random coupling, the Gaussian distribution can potentially serve as a robust spectral indicator of criticality. Remarkably, the spectral density is well-described by Tsallis statistics, with the entropic index $q$ evolving from $q = -1$ (semicircle, $T=\infty$) to $q = 1$ (Gaussian) at $T_c$, revealing a statistical structure inside the paramagnetic phase. We find $q\le 1$ within numerical precision. While the local level statistics remain consistent with GOE statistics, reflecting standard level repulsion, the temperature dependence appears mainly in the global spectral density. Our results present spectral statistics as a computationally efficient complement to multi-replica correlator methods and provide a new perspective on cooperative and critical phenomena in disordered systems.

*Zhiyu Cao,Peter G. Wolynes*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究在随机一级相变理论框架下，分析了驱动非晶系统近失稳时的热雪崩统计特性，揭示了非泊松等待时间统计和非马尔可夫老化动力学，并推导了雪崩幅度和计数的完整分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用弦状激发（stringy excitations）描述非泊松等待时间统计，并将其嵌入广义主方程（generalized Master equation）以捕捉雪崩簇的非马尔可夫老化动力学；应用全计数统计（full counting statistics）分析准静态剪切和随机振动两种驱动协议下的雪崩分布。

Result: 研究揭示了热雪崩的非泊松等待时间统计特性，广义主方程成功捕捉了雪崩簇的非马尔可夫老化动力学；通过全计数统计推导出了雪崩幅度和雪崩计数的完整分布，并分析了其中间时间行为。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了分析驱动非晶系统热雪崩统计特性的理论框架，揭示了其非平衡特征和动力学行为，为理解玻璃态系统的非平衡统计力学提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: Within the framework of the random first-order transition theory of glasses, we discuss the statistics of thermal avalanches, the large scale rearrangements in driven amorphous systems near their instability. Stringy excitations yield nonPoisson waiting time statistics. Embedding these statistics in a generalized Master equation captures the nonMarkovian, aging dynamics of avalanche clusters. We apply this framework to analyze nonequilibrium signatures of thermal avalanches, auto correlation functions and effective temperatures, under both quasi static shear and stochastic shaking protocols. We use full counting statistics to derive the complete distribution of both the avalanche magnitudes and avalanche counts, uncovering the intermediate time behavior.

### [155] [Non-equilibrium dynamics of the disordered Power of Two model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04220)
*Kunal Singh,Sayan Choudhury*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有幂次二（PWR2）长程相互作用的可编程自旋模型的非平衡动力学，发现强无序会抑制信息传播并诱导局域化，但系统在热力学极限下对任何有限无序强度仍保持遍历性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于近期实验实现了具有长程相互作用的可编程自旋模型，特别是针对幂次二（Power-of-Two, PWR2）模型的非平衡动力学。该模型包含稀疏的长程耦合，自旋间距离为 $d = 2^n$。

Method: 通过分析生存概率（survival probability）、半链纠缠熵（half-chain entanglement entropy）和时序关联器（out-of-time-ordered correlators, OTOCs）的时间演化来探索无序的影响。通过谱统计（spectral statistics）和本征态纠缠（eigenstate entanglement）提取临界无序强度 $h_c$ 以表征局域化转变。

Result: 足够强的无序会抑制信息传播并诱导局域化。在强无序区域，OTOCs 显示出由相互作用内在非局域性引起的非单调空间分布，表明与常规长程相互作用系统相比具有本质不同的信息混洗动力学。临界无序强度 $h_c$ 随系统尺寸增加而增大，且在固定无序强度下，本征态平均纠缠熵随系统尺寸增加而增加，而逆参与率（inverse participation ratio）减小，表明较大尺寸下退局域化增强。

Conclusion: 这些结果共同表明，幂次二（PWR2）模型在热力学极限下对于任何有限无序强度仍保持遍历性（ergodic）。

Abstract: Motivated by recent experimental realizations of programmable spin models with long-range interactions, we investigate the non-equilibrium dynamics of the Power-of-Two (PWR2) model. This model consists of sparse long-range couplings between spin-$1/2$ objects separated by $d = 2^n$. In the absence of disorder, the system exhibits rapid scrambling and fast thermalization. We explore the impact of disorder in this system by analyzing the time evolution of the survival probability, half-chain entanglement entropy, and out-of-time-ordered correlators (OTOCs). We find that sufficiently strong disorder suppresses information spreading and induces localization. Remarkably, in the strong-disorder regime, the OTOCs display a non-monotonic spatial profile arising from the intrinsic nonlocality of the interactions, signaling qualitatively distinct scrambling dynamics compared to conventional long-range interacting systems. To characterize the localization transition, we extract the critical disorder strength $h_c$ from the spectral statistics and the eigenstate entanglement. We observe that $h_c$ increases with system size. Furthermore, at a fixed disorder strength, the eigenstate-averaged entanglement entropy increases with system size, while the inverse participation ratio decreases, indicating enhanced delocalization at larger sizes. These results collectively suggest that the PWR2 model remains ergodic in the thermodynamic limit for any finite disorder strength.

</details>


### [156] [Predicting oscillations in complex networks with delayed feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04251)
*Shijie Liu,Jinliang Han,Tim Rogers,Yongzheng Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究系统探讨了结构复杂性与延迟反馈如何共同诱导复杂系统中的振荡动力学，提出了结合理论降维与数据驱动预测的分析框架，并通过电子电路实验验证了理论预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 振荡动力学是复杂网络的常见特征，在调节功能中发挥重要作用。从基因调控网络到生态系统，延迟反馈机制是系统尺度振荡的关键驱动因素，但由于高维性、非线性和延迟的结合，这类动力学的分析与预测极具挑战性。

Method: 研究引入了一个包含理论降维（theoretical dimension reduction）和数据驱动预测（data-driven prediction）的分析框架。通过可编程电子电路实验进行实证检验，并部署储层计算（reservoir computing）管道直接从时间序列数据准确预测振荡的发生。

Result: 研究发现振荡源于结构复杂性与延迟的相互作用，降维模型揭示了其临界阈值，并显示更大的连接性降低了振荡发生所需的延迟。实验观察到一旦结构复杂性和反馈延迟超过理论预测的临界阈值，就会产生振荡。

Conclusion: 该研究深化了对振荡调控的理解，并为预测复杂网络中的动力学提供了新途径。研究结果表明结构复杂性与延迟反馈的协同作用是产生系统尺度振荡的关键机制。

Abstract: Oscillatory dynamics are common features of complex networks, often playing essential roles in regulating function. Across scales from gene regulatory networks to ecosystems, delayed feedback mechanisms are key drivers of system-scale oscillations. The analysis and prediction of such dynamics are highly challenging, however, due to the combination of high-dimensionality, non-linearity and delay. Here, we systematically investigate how structural complexity and delayed feedback jointly induce oscillatory dynamics in complex systems, and introduce an analytic framework comprising theoretical dimension reduction and data-driven prediction. We reveal that oscillations emerge from the interplay of structural complexity and delay, with reduced models uncovering their critical thresholds and showing that greater connectivity lowers the delay required for their onset. Our theory is empirically tested in an experiment on a programmable electronic circuit, where oscillations are observed once structural complexity and feedback delay exceeded the critical thresholds predicted by our theory. Finally, we deploy a reservoir computing pipeline to accurately predict the onset of oscillations directly from timeseries data. Our findings deepen understanding of oscillatory regulation and offer new avenues for predicting dynamics in complex networks.

</details>

### [157] [Star-exponential for Fermi systems and the Feynman-Kac formula](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03558)
*J. Berra-Montiel,H. García-Compeán,A. Kafuri,A. Molgado*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于玻色系统星指数与量子传播子关系的形式体系，将其扩展到费米系统，建立了费米星指数与传播子的闭式表达式，并推导了费米版本的Feynman-Kac公式，为费米系统相空间研究提供了新的计算工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受玻色系统中星指数（star-exponential）与量子传播子关系的形式体系启发，本研究旨在将类似扩展应用于费米系统。具体动机是在形变量子化（deformation quantization）框架下，解决费米系统星指数（即演化算符的符号）的计算问题。

Method: 采用Grassmann变量和相干态（coherent states）方法，以获得费米星指数与其关联传播子的闭式表达式。通过该形式体系推导了费米版本的Feynman-Kac公式，并应用于简谐和受驱费米振子（Fermi oscillators）进行验证。

Result: 成功建立了费米星指数与传播子之间的明确关系，并推导出费米版本的Feynman-Kac公式，使得基态能量在相空间中的计算变得直接。方法在简谐和受驱费米振子中得到成功验证，为费米系统研究提供了有效的替代计算工具。

Conclusion: 本研究将玻色系统的星指数-传播子形式体系扩展到费米系统，建立了完整的费米形变量子化计算框架。所发展的方法为费米系统相空间研究提供了强大的替代计算工具，特别是在基态能量计算方面具有显著优势。

Abstract: Inspired by the formalism that relates the star-exponential with the quantum propagator for bosonic systems, in this work we introduce the analogous extension for the fermionic case. In particular, we analyse the problem of calculating the star-exponential (i.e., the symbol of the evolution operator) for Fermi systems within the deformation quantization program. Grassmann variables and coherent states are considered in order to obtain a closed-form expression for the fermionic star-exponential in terms of its associated propagator. As a primary application, a fermionic version of the Feynman-Kac formula is derived within this formalism, thus allowing a straightforward calculation of the ground state energy in phase space. Finally, the method is validated by successfully applying it to the simple harmonic and driven Fermi oscillators, for which the results developed here provide a powerful alternative computational tool for the study of fermionic systems.

</details>


### [158] [(Quantum) reference frames, relational observables, gauge reduction and physical interpretation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04072)
*Thomas Thiemann*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了广义相对论等规范系统中参考系的操作性定义、量子化路径选择以及关系参考系变换（RRFT）等核心概念，旨在解决规范理论中观测量的物理诠释问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在广义相对论等规范系统中，时空坐标受时空微分同胚（spacetime diffeomorphisms）规范变换影响而成为非可观测量，这促使研究者需要操作性定义物质参考系（material reference frames），通过物质或几何参考场来指定坐标，从而建立关系可观测量（relational observables）、关系参考系（relational reference frames）和规范约化（gauge reduction）的概念框架。

Method: 论文采用非微扰场论（non-perturbative field theory）框架，具有足够普适性以涵盖广义相对论耦合标准物质的情形。核心方法是推导关系参考系变换（relational reference frame transformation, RRFT）的一般公式，并系统探究其性质。

Result: 研究推导了关系参考系变换（RRFT）的一般公式，并深入探索了其性质。该框架为解决量子化前后规范约化路径选择、参考场量子化方式、不同量子参考系间关系等核心问题提供了理论基础。

Conclusion: 该概念性工作系统性地解决了规范理论中参考系操作性定义、量子化路径及其物理诠释等关键问题，为广义相对论等规范系统的量子化提供了关系参考系变换（RRFT）这一核心工具，深化了对量子参考系相对性本质的理解。

Abstract: It is mandatory to know how to operationally define and translate a reference frame into mathematics, in order that a physical interpretation of theory calculations in terms of observational data is possible. The situation is particularly challenging for gauge systems such as General Relativity where spacetime coordinates are subject to spacetime diffeomorphisms considered as gauge transformations turning coordinates into non-observables. This motivates the idea of operationally defined (material) reference frames which specify coordinates in terms of matter or geometry reference fields leading to the concept of relational observables, relational reference frames and gauge reduction. Upon quantisation, all fields become operator valued distributions. Now new conceptual and technical questions arise such as: Should one reduce before or after quantisation and how are the reference fields quantised respectively in either route? Is a reference frame itself subject to quantisation and how are different quantum reference frames related? How does the gauge reduction fit into this, i.e. how can it be that a certain reference field is considered a non-observable in one reference frame and an observable in another which upon quantisation even displays fluctuations? How precisely are gauge dependent fields interpreted in terms of the relational observables in a given reference frame? What is the relative dynamics, e.g. how exactly are physical Hamiltonians of two relational reference frames related? The present conceptual work addresses these and related questions in a non-perturbative field theory context of sufficient generality to cover General Relativity coupled to standard matter. A central role is played by the concept of the relational reference frame transformation (RRFT) for which a general formula is derived and its properties are explored.

</details>


### [159] [Bayesian post-correction of non-Markovian errors in multi-mode bosonic gravimetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03426)
*Bharath Hebbe Madhusudhana,Andrew Harter,Avadh Saxena*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在随机空间不均匀性存在下，利用玻色囚禁原子进行重力测量的误差校正方法。通过贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference）进行后校正，并定义了有效费舍尔信息（effective Fisher information）来量化测量精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于解决随机空间不均匀性（random spatial inhomogeneity）对玻色囚禁原子重力测量造成的量子非马尔可夫误差（quantum non-Markovian errors）。这些误差限制了重力测量的精度，需要开发有效的后处理校正方法。

Method: 采用贝叶斯推断进行误差后校正，通过原位测量误差并根据测量结果优化数据处理。定义了有效费舍尔信息 $F_{\text{eff}}$ 来量化测量精度，并分析了其与原子数 $N$ 和模式数 $L$ 的标度关系。

Result: 当模式数 $L<\ell+2$（$\ell$ 为独立误差源数量）时，有效费舍尔信息标度为 $F_{\text{eff}} \sim \frac{N^2}{a+bN^2}$，最终趋于常数。当 $L\geq \ell+2$ 时，通过希尔伯特空间优化可获得海森堡标度 $F_{\text{eff}}= O(N^2)$，且几乎任何 Haar 随机态都具有此标度。

Conclusion: 研究提出了一种类似洛施密特回波（Loschmidt echo-like）的实验序列用于误差缓解的重力测量和梯度测量，并指出有效费舍尔信息可解释为对应等效非厄米演化（non-Hermitian evolution）的费舍尔信息。

Abstract: We study gravimetry with bosonic trapped atoms in the presence of random spatial inhomogeneity. The errors resulting from a random, shot-to-shot fluctuating spatial inhomogeneity are quantum non-Markovian. We show that in a system with $L>2$ modes (i.e., trapping sites), these errors can be post-corrected using a Bayesian inference. The post-correction is done via in situ measurements of the errors and refining the data-processing according to the measured error. We define an effective Fisher information $F_{\text{eff}}$ for such measurements with a Bayesian post-correction and show that the Cramer-Rao bound for the final precision is $\frac{1}{\sqrt{F_{\text{eff}}}}$. Exploring the scaling of the effective Fisher information with the number of atoms $N$, we show that it saturates to a constant when there are too many sources of error and too few modes. That is, with $\ell$ independent sources of error, we show that the effective Fisher information scales as $F_{\text{eff}} \sim \frac{N^2}{a+bN^2}$ for constants $a, b>0$ when the number of modes is small: $L<\ell+2$, even after maximization over the Hilbert space. With larger number of modes, $L\geq \ell+2$, we show that the effective Fisher information has a Heisenberg scaling $F_{\text{eff}}= O(N^2)$ when optimized over the Hilbert space. Finally, we study the density of the effective Fisher information in the Hilbert space and show that when $L\geq \ell+2$, almost any Haar random state has a Heisenberg scaling, i.e., $F_{\text{eff}}=O(N^2)$. Based on these results, we develop a Loschmidt echo-like experimental sequence for error mitigated gravimetry and gradiometry and discuss potential implementations. Finally, we argue that the effective Fisher information can be interpreted as the Fisher information corresponding to an equivalent non-Hertimitian evolution.

</details>


### [160] [O-Sensing: Operator Sensing for Interaction Geometry and Symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03826)
*Meng Ye-Ming,Shi Zhe-Yu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: O-Sensing协议通过简约性优化从量子多体系统的低能本征态中提取哈密顿量和对称性，无需先验的相互作用几何信息。该方法在Erdős-Rényi图上的海森堡模型中成功重建了相互作用几何并发现了额外的长程守恒算符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索是否能够仅从量子多体系统的少数低能本征态推断其哈密顿量、相互作用几何和对称性，而无需预先知道哪些位点之间存在相互作用。直接求解本征值方程会产生高度简并的候选算符子空间，使得局部哈密顿量被隐藏在大量守恒量中，从而模糊了相互作用几何。

Method: O-Sensing协议采用简约性驱动优化（parsimony-driven optimization）从简并子空间中提取最大稀疏的算符基。然后通过最大化采样子空间内的谱熵（spectral entropy）来选择哈密顿量，这实质上最小化了简并度。该方法在连通Erdős-Rényi图上的海森堡模型（Heisenberg models）上进行验证。

Result: O-Sensing成功重建了相互作用几何并发现了额外的长程守恒算符。研究建立了跨图密度的可学习性相图（learnability phase diagram），其中包含一个显著的"混淆"区域（confusion regime），在该区域简约性倾向于补图（complement graph）上的对偶描述。

Conclusion: 结果表明，稀疏性优化能够将相互作用几何重建为涌现输出，使得从低能本征态中同时恢复哈密顿量及其对称性成为可能。这为从量子态数据推断系统基本性质提供了一种新方法。

Abstract: We ask whether the Hamiltonian, interaction geometry, and symmetries of a quantum many-body system can be inferred from a few low-lying eigenstates without knowing which sites interact with each other. Directly solving the eigenvalue equations imposes constraints that yield a highly degenerate subspace of candidate operators, where the local Hamiltonian is hidden among an extensive family of conserved quantities, obscuring the interaction geometry. Here we introduce O-Sensing, a protocol designed to extract the Hamiltonian and symmetries directly from these states. Specifically, O-Sensing employs parsimony-driven optimization to extract a maximally sparse operator basis from the degenerate subspace. The Hamiltonian is then selected from this basis by maximizing spectral entropy (effectively minimizing degeneracy) within the sampled subspace. We validate O-Sensing on Heisenberg models on connected Erdős--Rényi graphs, where it reconstructs the interaction geometry and uncovers additional long-range conserved operators. We establish a learnability phase diagram across graph densities, featuring a pronounced ``confusion'' regime where parsimony favors a dual description on the complement graph. These results show that sparsity optimization can reconstruct interaction geometry as an emergent output, enabling simultaneous recovery of the Hamiltonian and its symmetries from low-energy eigenstates.

</details>


### [161] [Fractional topology in open systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03854)
*Xi Wu,Xiang Zhang,Fuxiang Li*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在增益和损耗作用下周期性Su-Schrieffer-Heeger链中分数拓扑不变量的涌现，揭示了通过调节量子跳跃算符参数或时间演化中的动力学转变，整数拓扑不变量可转变为分数拓扑不变量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解开放量子系统中分数拓扑（fractional topology）的涌现机制，特别是在周期性Su-Schrieffer-Heeger链中，当系统受到增益和损耗作用时，整数拓扑不变量如何转变为分数拓扑不变量。

Method: 采用Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad主方程描述增益和损耗，通过调节量子跳跃算符（jump operators）参数或观察时间演化中的动力学转变，研究拓扑不变量的变化；最后提出在具有分数填充的长程跳跃光子晶格中通过布洛赫态层析成像进行观测。

Result: 研究发现分数拓扑不变量不再具有传统意义上的量子化拓扑性质，但通过将布里渊区扩展至覆盖多个周期，总绕数可重新获得整数量子化；同时展示了在具有分数填充的长程跳跃光子晶格中通过布洛赫态层析成像观测此类效应的可能性。

Conclusion: 该研究为理解开放量子系统中的分数拓扑现象开辟了新途径，揭示了在非厄米系统中拓扑不变量的分数化转变机制及其观测方法。

Abstract: We investigate the emergence of fractional topological invariants in a periodic Su-Schrieffer- Heeger chain subject to gain and loss, governed by the Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad master equations. After preparing the symmetry condition for integer topological invariants, we investigate their transition to fractional ones in steady states, which can happen either by tuning parameters in jump operators or as a dynamical transition during time evolution. Moreover, we show that these fractional topological invariants no longer possess quantized topology in the conventional sense. However, by extending the Brillouin zone to cover multiple cycles, the total winding regains integer quantization. Finally, we show how such effects can be observed in long-range hopping photonic lattices with fractional fillings, via Bloch state tomography. Our results open a new pathway to understand fractional topology in open quantum systems.

</details>


### [162] [Many-Body Structural Effects in Periodically Driven Quantum Batteries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03883)
*Rohit Kumar Shukla,Cheng Shang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了多体量子电池在周期性驱动下的充电性能由系统结构特征决定，包括相互作用范围、边界条件、系统尺寸和可积性。研究发现长程相互作用和非可积性是实现快速、可扩展且鲁棒充电的关键资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子电池在静态驱动下已被广泛研究，但在周期性驱动下的多体系统中其性能仍远未得到充分理解。本研究旨在揭示多体结构如何从根本上决定集体自旋-1/2量子电池在周期性伊辛充电器驱动下的充电性能。

Method: 研究分析了周期性伊辛充电器驱动的集体自旋-1/2量子电池系统。通过考察相互作用范围、边界条件、系统尺寸和可积性等结构特征，系统研究了这些因素如何影响存储能量和充电功率。特别关注了连通性标度、边界几何以及可积性在周期性驱动下的作用。

Result: 长程相互作用充电器表现出超广延能量存储，在广泛的驱动周期和系统尺寸范围内接近理论上限。相比之下，最近邻充电器仅在精细调谐的共度条件下实现最优充电。开放边界条件比周期性边界条件更具鲁棒性。非可积性通过抑制守恒量并促进遍历弗洛凯动力学来增强能量存储，从而实现多体能谱的有效布居。

Conclusion: 长程非可积性是实现集体量子电池快速、可扩展且鲁棒充电的核心资源。研究阐明了如何利用多体系统的结构特征与周期性驱动相结合，实现高效的集体充电动力学。

Abstract: While quantum batteries have been widely studied under static driving, their performance under periodic driving in many-body systems remains far less understood. In this Letter, we uncover structural principles showing that many-body structure fundamentally determines the charging performance of a collective spin-1/2 quantum battery driven by a periodic Ising charger. In particular, interaction range, boundary conditions, system size, and integrability -- capturing graph connectivity, geometry, even-odd effects, and many-body dynamics -- emerge as critical factors for enhancing stored energy and charging power. First, we analyze how connectivity scaling and boundary geometry shape battery performance. We show that long-range interacting chargers exhibit superextensive energy storage, approaching the fundamental upper bound over broad ranges of driving periods and system sizes. In contrast, nearest-neighbor chargers achieve optimal charging only under finely tuned commensurability conditions. Moreover, we find that open boundary conditions (OBC) enhance robustness compared to periodic boundary conditions (PBC). Second, we examine the role of integrability under periodic driving. We demonstrate that nonintegrability enhances energy storage by suppressing conserved quantities and promoting ergodic Floquet dynamics, thereby enabling efficient population of the many-body spectrum. Through systematic structural optimization across multiple parameters, we identify long-range nonintegrability as a central resource for fast, scalable, and robust charging of collective quantum batteries. Our results clarify how structural features of many-body systems, together with periodic driving, can be harnessed to achieve efficient collective charging dynamics.

</details>


### [163] [Fermi-Dirac thermal measurements: A framework for quantum hypothesis testing and semidefinite optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04061)
*Nana Liu,Mark M. Wilde*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出将量子测量算符的特征值约束类比于泡利不相容原理，从而将量子假设检验中的测量算符解释为有效费米子模式。通过最小化费米子自由能，作者引入了费米-狄拉克热测量（Fermi-Dirac thermal measurements）作为优化测量，并建立了费米-狄拉克机（Fermi-Dirac machines）这一新的量子机器学习模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子测量是从量子态中恢复编码信息的关键手段，在量子假设检验（quantum hypothesis testing）中尤为重要。传统方法需要寻找最优测量以获得正确结论，但这一过程面临数学约束和计算挑战。

Method: 作者注意到量子测量算符的特征值约束与泡利不相容原理（Pauli exclusion principle）对费米子的约束相同，从而将测量算符的每个特征模式解释为独立的有效费米子模式。通过固定温度并最小化总期望费米子自由能（fermionic free energy），推导出费米-狄拉克热测量作为优化测量的形式。

Result: 在低温极限下，费米-狄拉克热测量的性能近似于量子假设检验的最优测量。作者展示了其参数可通过经典或混合量子-经典优化算法学习，从而建立了费米-狄拉克机这一新的量子机器学习模型，作为基于热态的量子玻尔兹曼机（quantum Boltzmann machines）的替代方案。

Conclusion: 该方法不仅适用于量子假设检验，还可推广到一般半定优化问题（semidefinite optimization problems），为量子计算机上的半定优化提供了新范式：目标是实现热测量而非制备热态。作者还提出了实现费米-狄拉克热测量的量子算法以及二阶混合量子-经典优化算法。

Abstract: Quantum measurements are the means by which we recover messages encoded into quantum states. They are at the forefront of quantum hypothesis testing, wherein the goal is to perform an optimal measurement for arriving at a correct conclusion. Mathematically, a measurement operator is Hermitian with eigenvalues in [0,1]. By noticing that this constraint on each eigenvalue is the same as that imposed on fermions by the Pauli exclusion principle, we interpret every eigenmode of a measurement operator as an independent effective fermionic mode. Under this perspective, various objective functions in quantum hypothesis testing can be viewed as the total expected energy associated with these fermionic occupation numbers. By instead fixing a temperature and minimizing the total expected fermionic free energy, we find that optimal measurements for these modified objective functions are Fermi-Dirac thermal measurements, wherein their eigenvalues are specified by Fermi-Dirac distributions. In the low-temperature limit, their performance closely approximates that of optimal measurements for quantum hypothesis testing, and we show that their parameters can be learned by classical or hybrid quantum-classical optimization algorithms. This leads to a new quantum machine-learning model, termed Fermi-Dirac machines, consisting of parameterized Fermi-Dirac thermal measurements-an alternative to quantum Boltzmann machines based on thermal states. Beyond hypothesis testing, we show how general semidefinite optimization problems can be solved using this approach, leading to a novel paradigm for semidefinite optimization on quantum computers, in which the goal is to implement thermal measurements rather than prepare thermal states. Finally, we propose quantum algorithms for implementing Fermi-Dirac thermal measurements, and we also propose second-order hybrid quantum-classical optimization algorithms.

</details>


### [164] [Constructing Arbitrary Coherent Rearrangements in Optical Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04210)
*Alexander Roth,Liyang Qiu,Timon Hilker,Titus Franz,Philipp M. Preiss*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种在光学晶格中实现超冷原子相干重排的方案，利用光学超晶格动力学与离散线性光学的类比，通过Clemenets方案系统构建任意全局N维单粒子幺正变换，实现可编程的量子动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光学晶格中超冷原子运动自由度的相干控制为实现可编程的量子动力学提供了有前景的途径。该研究旨在实现超冷原子的相干重排，对应单粒子运动态的任意幺正变换。

Method: 利用光学超晶格（optical superlattices）动力学与离散线性光学（discrete linear optics）的类比，采用Clemenets方案系统地从双阱阵列中的隧穿（tunneling）和相移（phase shifts）构建任意全局N维单粒子幺正变换。隧穿全局控制，而局部操作通过位点分辨的势能偏移（site-resolved potential shifts）实现。

Result: 数值研究了该方案对强度噪声和寻址串扰（addressing crosstalk）的敏感性。识别了由该幺正构造实现的关键子程序，包括离散傅里叶变换（Discrete Fourier Transform）和非原生哈密顿量（non-native Hamiltonians）的实现。将该方案扩展到二维可实现全对全原子重排，其电路深度随原子数亚线性（sublinearly）增长。

Conclusion: 该方案提供了一种高密度且高度可扩展的原子重排方法，光学晶格中超冷原子的相干重排为实现可编程的量子动力学开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Coherent control of motional degrees of freedom of ultracold atoms in optical lattices offers a promising route towards programmable quantum dynamics with massive particles. We propose and analyze a scheme for implementing coherent rearrangement of ultracold atoms, corresponding to arbitrary unitary transformations on single-particle motional states. Exploiting an analogy between dynamics in optical superlattices and discrete linear optics, we employ the Clements scheme to systematically construct any global $N$-dimensional single-particle unitary from tunneling and phase shifts in arrays of double wells. Tunneling is controlled globally, while local operations are achieved through site-resolved potential shifts. We numerically investigate the susceptibility of the scheme to intensity noise and addressing crosstalk. We identify key subroutines enabled by this unitary construction, including the Discrete Fourier Transform and the implementation of non-native Hamiltonians. Extending the scheme to two dimensions enables all-to-all atomic rearrangement with a circuit depth that scales sublinearly with the atom number, providing a high-density and highly scalable approach to atom rearrangement.

</details>


### [165] [Dynamical Behaviour of Density Correlations Across the Chaotic Phase for Interacting Bosons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04373)
*Óscar Dueñas,Alberto Rodríguez*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究一维玻色-哈伯德（Bose-Hubbard）模型中两点密度关联的传播，通过关联输运距离（CTD）这一实验可测量表征关联在时空中的扩展。研究发现可积极限下CTD呈弹道增长，而混沌相的出现导致明显的亚弹道区域，但关联前沿在所有相互作用强度下均保持弹道传播。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究一维玻色-哈伯德模型在热力学极限下两点密度关联的传播特性。研究动机在于通过关联输运距离（correlation transport distance, CTD）这一实验可测量，深入理解关联在时空中的扩展行为，超越简单的光锥图像描述。

Method: 研究方法基于对一维玻色-哈伯德哈密顿量的分析，重点关注关联输运距离（CTD）这一表征关联空间扩展的物理量。通过细致分析时空关联剖面，研究不同相互作用强度下的关联传播特性。

Result: 研究确认模型的可积极限（integrable limits）表现出CTD的弹道增长（ballistic growth），而混沌相（chaotic phase）的出现导致明显的亚弹道区域（sub-ballistic regime）。然而，关联前沿在所有相互作用强度下均保持弹道传播，CTD的混沌诱导减速源于长时间距离依赖关联尾迹的出现以及关联前沿振幅的增强衰减。

Conclusion: 本文提供了超越简单光锥图像的关联输运详细表征。研究结果表明，虽然混沌相导致CTD的亚弹道行为，但关联前沿在所有情况下均保持弹道传播，揭示了关联传播的复杂动力学特性。

Abstract: We investigate the propagation of two-point density correlations in the one-dimensional Bose-Hubbard Hamiltonian in the thermodynamic limit in terms of the correlation transport distance (CTD), an experimentally measurable magnitude that characterizes the spatial spreading of correlations in time. We confirm that the integrable limits of the model exhibit CTD ballistic growth, while the onset of the chaotic phase leads to the emergence of a pronounced sub-ballistic regime, in agreement with previous results for finite systems. By a meticulous analysis of the spatio-temporal correlation profiles, we show that the correlation front nonetheless propagates ballistically for all interaction strengths, and that the chaos-induced slowdown of the CTD originates from the emergence of long-time distance-dependent correlation tails, together with an enhanced decay of the correlation front amplitude. Our results thus provide a detailed characterization of correlation transport that goes beyond a simple light-cone picture.

</details>

### [166] [Quantum anomaly for benchmarking quantum computing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03697)
*Tomoya Hayata,Arata Yamamoto*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 该研究利用规范理论中轴反常（axial anomaly）的微扰精确性，提出将其作为量子模拟的验证基准，并在离子阱量子计算机上成功模拟了晶格规范理论中的反常轴荷产生。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着量子计算硬件的快速发展，建立验证量子计算正确性的系统策略变得日益重要。该研究旨在利用规范理论中轴反常的精确特性，为量子模拟提供非平凡的验证基准。

Method: 研究提出将轴反常作为晶格规范理论量子模拟的验证测试，并在名为"Reimei"的离子阱量子计算机上模拟了${\mathbb Z}_N$晶格规范理论中的反常轴荷产生。通过取U(1)极限、无穷小时间极限和无限体积极限，验证了模拟结果。

Result: 在未使用误差缓解技术的情况下，研究成功在统计不确定度范围内再现了反常系数。结果表明，轴反常可以在当前量子计算机上进行模拟，并可作为量子计算的验证测试。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了轴反常可以在现有量子计算机上模拟，并可作为验证量子计算正确性的有效基准，为量子模拟的验证提供了新策略。

Abstract: Given the rapid advances in quantum computing hardware, establishing systematic strategies for verifying the correctness of quantum computations has become increasingly important. Exploiting the fact that the axial anomaly in gauge theories is exact to all orders in perturbation theory, we propose the axial anomaly as a nontrivial benchmark for quantum simulations of lattice gauge theories. We simulate anomalous axial-charge production in ${\mathbb Z}_N$ lattice gauge theories on the trapped-ion quantum computer ``Reimei''. After taking the U(1), infinitesimal time, and infinite volume limits, we successfully reproduce the anomaly coefficient within statistical uncertainties, even without error mitigation. Our results demonstrate that the axial anomaly can be simulated on current quantum computers and serves as a verification test of quantum computations.

</details>


### [167] [Lattice extraction of the Collins-Soper kernel using the auxiliary field representation of the Wilson line](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03814)
*Anthony Francis,C. -J. David Lin,Wayne Morris,Yong Zhao*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 该研究提出在格点（lattice）上通过一维辅助费米子场（auxiliary fermion fields）构建Wilson线，从而从TMD软函数（soft function）中提取Collins-Soper（CS）核。研究在对应于Minkowski空间中"类空"（spacelike）区域的格点区域进行，探索了两种方法：可获得软函数和CS核的"比值法"（ratio method），以及仅提取CS核但统计精度更高的"双比值法"（double ratio）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于通过格点QCD方法精确计算Collins-Soper核，该核在横向动量依赖（TMD）因子化中起关键作用。通过在格点上构建Wilson线的一维辅助费米子场表示，为从TMD软函数中提取CS核提供了新的计算框架。

Method: 采用两种主要方法：1）"比值法"（ratio method），可同时获得软函数和CS核；2）"双比值法"（double ratio），仅提取CS核但能达到更高的统计精度。计算在对应于Minkowski空间"类空"区域（Collins方案）的格点区域进行，通过将复辅助场方向矢量映射到Wilson线快度（rapidity）实现与Minkowski空间的匹配。

Result: 研究展示了使用"双比值法"对CS核的初步提取结果，该方法能够实现高统计精度的计算。通过将格点计算中的复辅助场方向矢量映射到Wilson线快度，成功建立了与Minkowski空间物理的对应关系。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了在格点上通过一维辅助费米子场方法计算Collins-Soper核的可行框架，提供了两种不同精度和应用场景的计算方法。初步结果表明"双比值法"在统计精度方面具有优势，为后续更精确的CS核格点计算奠定了基础。

Abstract: The Collins-Soper (CS) kernel may be obtained through the TMD soft function by formulating the Wilson line in terms of 1-dimensional auxiliary fermion fields on the lattice. Our computation takes place in the region of the lattice that corresponds to the "spacelike" region in Minkowski space, i.e., Collins' scheme. We explore two methods for obtaining the CS kernel. The "ratio method"; which would allow us to obtain the soft function as well as the CS kernel. And the "double ratio"; which allows us to achieve a high degree of statistical precision, but only produces the CS kernel. The matching of our result to Minkowski space is achieved through the mapping of the complex auxiliary field directional vector to the Wilson line rapidity. We present a preliminary extraction of the CS kernel using the "double ratio", and discuss the methodology employed.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文采用了晶格计算（lattice calculation）方法，具体介绍了布达佩斯-马赛-伍珀塔尔（Budapest-Marseille-Wuppertal, BMW）和DMZ合作组的最新结果。该方法通过混合确定（hybrid determination）强子真空极化（hadronic vacuum polarisation）贡献，达到了0.45%的精度。

I will present the latest results from the Budapest-Marseille-Wuppertal (BMW) and DMZ collaborations, with a hybrid determination of the hadronic vacuum polarisation contribution to a precision of 0.45%

### [169] [Grid-agnostic volume of fluid approach with interface sharpening and surface tension for compressible multiphase flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04270)
*J. Marziale,J. Sun,D. Salac,J. Chen*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种适用于任意网格的多相流界面锐化方法，通过构建反扩散体积体力实现界面保持，验证了与Young-Laplace条件的良好一致性，并展示了表面张力与界面锐化协同作用下复杂形状的恢复能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多相流有限体积法（FVM）离散化产生的界面扩散需要锐化机制，现有方法主要针对结构化四边形网格，但工程应用常需适应不规则几何形状的网格设计。因此需要开发可推广至任意构造网格的通用界面锐化方法。

Method: 将界面锐化构建为反扩散体积体力（ant-idiffusive volumetric body force），其大小在单元中心根据局部可压缩流动特性和单元邻域几何推导。流动模型采用基于AUSM+up的方法进行通量评估，并对每种流体施加刚性状态方程以闭合线性系统并提取辅助变量。

Result: 验证测试显示与Young-Laplace条件良好一致，界面收敛到压力跳跃与界面力平衡对应的解析解。进一步结果表明，通过表面张力与界面锐化的联合作用，可从高度变化曲率的形状恢复圆形。剪切驱动液滴夹断结果在不同Weber-Ohnesorge数组合下与文献提供的液滴形状良好吻合。

Conclusion: 本研究成功开发了适用于任意网格的通用界面锐化方法，通过反扩散体积体力机制有效保持多相流界面清晰度，验证了其在复杂几何和流动条件下的鲁棒性和准确性。

Abstract: The interfacial diffusion associated with finite volume method (FVM) discretizations of multiphase flows creates the need for an interface sharpening mechanism. Such solutions for structured quadrilateral grids are well documented, but various engineering applications require mesh designs specific to the irregular geometry of the physical system it is modeling. Therefore this study casts interface sharpening as an ant-idiffusive volumetric body force whose calculation procedure is generalizable to an arbitrarily constructed grid. The force magnitude is derived at cell centers as a function of the local compressible flow characteristics and the geometry of the cell neighborhood. The flow model uses an AUSM+up based method for flux evaluation and imposes a stiffened equation of state onto each of the fluids in order to close the linear system and extract auxiliary variables. Validation tests show good agreement with the Young-Laplace condition whereby the interface converges to the analytical solution corresponding to a balance between a pressure jump and interfacial forces. Further results show the recovery of a circle starting from a shape with highly variational curvature through the combined effects of surface tension and interface sharpening. Lastly shear-driven droplet pinchoff results show good agreement with droplet shapes provided by the surrounding literature at various Weber-Ohnesorge number combinations.

</details>

### [170] [Advancing Food Nanotoxicology with Microphysiological Systems: Rebalancing the Risk/Benefit Ratio Toward Safer Nano-Enabled Food Innovations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03356)
*Georges Dubourg*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本综述评估了微生理系统（microphysiological systems, MPS）在纳米食品安全性评估中的应用潜力，特别关注肠道靶向MPS如何模拟胃肠道纳米颗粒暴露，以解决传统评估方法的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米材料在食品中的应用虽能延长保质期、提高安全性并改善品质，但其潜在毒性仍是关注焦点。传统体外和体内评估方法难以模拟胃肠道的复杂性，导致纳米毒性数据不一致且缺乏预测性，阻碍了对纳米食品的准确风险评估。

Method: 本综述通过评估微生理系统（MPS），特别是肠道靶向MPS的潜力，分析这些技术如何复制与食品特定风险评估相关的关键生理过程。采用比较分析方法探讨技术进步及其在纳米毒理学中的应用。

Result: 综述探讨了MPS技术如何模拟肠道屏障功能、微生物群-免疫相互作用以及肠道器官通讯等关键生理过程。通过比较分析，研究了MPS如何更好地适应纳米食品安全性评估的需求。

Conclusion: 微生理系统（MPS）为解决纳米食品风险评估中的现有局限性提供了有前景的途径，通过更生理相关的模型来改善纳米毒性数据的预测性和一致性，从而支持更准确的纳米食品安全评估。

Abstract: Incorporating nanomaterials into food products provides key benefits, including extended shelf life, improved safety, and enhanced quality and texture. These innovations could help tackle major challenges in modern food systems, such as reducing waste and enhancing food quality and safety. However, potential toxicity remains a concern, compounded by the lack of physiologically relevant models for assessing ingested nanomaterials. Traditional in vitro and in vivo approaches often fail to mimic gastrointestinal complexity, resulting in inconsistent and non predictive nanotoxicity data that hinder accurate risk assessment of nano enabled foods. To address this gap, this review evaluates the potential of microphysiological systems (MPS), particularly gut-targeted MPS, for modeling gastrointestinal nanoparticle exposure. It examines how MPS technologies replicate key physiological processes relevant to food specific risk assessment, including intestinal barrier function, microbiota immune interactions, and gut organ communication. A comparative analysis of technological advances and their applications in nanotoxicology explores how MPS can be better adapted for nanofood safety evaluation.

</details>
